The Northeast Problem and the League of Nations (101)

The Japanese Representative's Tone is Belligerent

Matsuoka said, "The Chinese representative has reserved the right to raise objections to the statements made at the next meeting. However, I would like to remind the Chinese representative that I am not asking them to debate the Tanaka Memorial. The document is a forgery, and there is no need to argue about it. But since the Chinese representative has made a definite accusation, they should provide evidence to substantiate their claim. I hope the Chinese representative will not forget my request at the next meeting."

The Chairman Invites Lord Lytton to Attend

At this point, the chairman invited Lord Lytton, head of the Commission of Enquiry, to attend. The chairman also said, "The members of the Executive Yuan have carefully listened to the speeches of the Chinese and Japanese representatives last Monday and this afternoon. The members of the Commission of Enquiry have also accepted the invitation of the Executive Yuan to attend and listen to the views of both sides. I am convinced that the members of the Executive Yuan are very concerned as to whether the members of the Commission of Enquiry, after hearing the statements of China and Japan, have any intention of adding to or amending the statements made in the report. If the members can agree, then I propose that the members of the Commission of Enquiry convene a meeting to consider this question and report their views to the Executive Yuan as quickly as possible within the scope of convenience. Can all members agree to this?"

"Matsuoka": "We do not object to the chairman's proposal, but what should be clearly acknowledged is that any opinion expressed should be the opinion of the Commission of Enquiry as a whole, and not the opinion of any individual member. Another point to note is that, in our view, the mission of the Commission of Enquiry was completed after it submitted its report to the Executive Yuan. Therefore, according to the task of the Commission, it is beyond the authority of the Commission to discuss or express opinions on the statements or memoranda issued by our government or by me."

"Chairman": "Regarding the first point raised by the Japanese representative, it should naturally be the opinion of the Commission of Enquiry as a whole. Regarding the second point, I believe that the Commission of Enquiry still exists until the Executive Yuan officially dissolves it. Therefore, if the Executive Yuan wishes to know the overall opinion of the Commission of Enquiry, it may as well consult it."

"Matsuoka": "I am afraid that the Chairman has misunderstood what I said. Page 138 of the Commission of Enquiry's report states, 'Our work is now complete.' We fully agree with this statement. The work of the Commission of Enquiry was completed when it completed its report. Therefore, we believe that the Commission has no right to make any criticisms or express any opinions on any events after the completion of the report. This is our position. If the Executive Yuan does not agree with this point, then I must express my disagreement and reserve our position."

"Chairman": "In my view, the work of the Commission of Enquiry should not be completed until the Executive Yuan has formally dissolved it. According to past practice, after any commission of enquiry is formed, its chairman often attends meetings of the Executive Yuan to answer questions, so as to explain various points in its report. There are already many such precedents."

"Yuan Representative": "I only represent the Chinese government in endorsing the chairman's proposal to invite the Commission of Enquiry to express its views. Since the representatives of China and Japan have already made lengthy statements in the Executive Yuan, especially the Japanese representative who has commented on the factual parts of the Commission of Enquiry's report, we should give the Commission of Enquiry an opportunity to express its views. However, I still have opinions on what the Japanese representative stated today, which I will express at the next meeting. It seems that the Commission's statement of opinion should wait until after I have finished expressing my opinion."

"Matsuoka": "I fully sympathize with the feelings expressed by the Chinese representative, but in order to avoid misunderstandings, I must state one point. In our view, the work of the Commission of Enquiry is completed after it has completed its report. Thereafter, it cannot express opinions or make criticisms. We must act according to the rules. If my interpretation is wrong, then I am willing to withdraw it. However, I still have significant doubts about this point."

"Chairman": "I would like to explain my proposal. I am not suggesting that the Commission of Enquiry should add to or change its report. However, I ask the members to meet and discuss whether they have any intention of changing or adding to the opinions stated in the report after they have heard the views of both China and Japan, and to report the facts to the Executive Yuan."

"Matsuoka": "This is what we object to. We have many doubts about this and must reserve the right to study it further."

"Lytton": Sir Lytton rose and said, "I would like to express, on behalf of my colleagues, our thanks to the Executive Yuan for giving us the opportunity to express whether we have any intention of adding to or changing our opinions in the report after hearing the statements of both China and Japan. However, since the opinion I express should be the opinion of the Commission of Enquiry as a whole, I cannot, of course, make any statement now until I have met with my colleagues to discuss it. We will meet tomorrow to discuss this point. As for the point raised by the Japanese representative, I dare say to the Japanese representative that after the members of the Commission of Enquiry returned to their countries, they did not meet, nor did they express opinions or take any action in the name of the Commission of Enquiry. As for the proposal of the Executive Yuan, it is not asking the Commission of Enquiry to criticize the statements made by the Chinese and Japanese representatives, but only asking them to express whether they have any changes to the opinions in the report."

"Chairman": "Apart from the reservation made by the Japanese representative, have the members of the Executive Yuan all agreed to my proposal?" (No one objects) (Debate completed on the 23rd) (To be continued)

Crisis of Commerce in Jiangxi Province

Exports Have Disappeared, Finance Has Lost Balance, Outwardly Strong but Inwardly Weak, the Trend of Defrauding is Extremely Prevalent

Nanchang Correspondence: Due to years of banditry in Jiangxi Province, the economy is withering, and the entire province's commerce is trending towards crisis. It has been found that the commerce of Jiangxi Province can be divided into three major parts: A. In terms of exports, (1) rice is the main export product of Jiangxi Province. In the past, exports were at least one million dan (a unit of dry measure), and the average price per dan was eight yuan, worth eight million yuan. Last year, due to bumper harvests in various provinces and the dumping of foreign rice, exports disappeared. Farmers are in dire straits, and rice merchants have suffered a setback. Even the Nanxun Railway and various transit stations have lost one million yuan in freight revenue. (2) Jingdezhen porcelain is sold all over the country and in overseas markets in Europe, America, Southeast Asia, and Japan. Last year, due to sluggish sales overseas and the government's implementation of production and sales taxes, there were no sales from March to August. In October, after it was changed to an annual business tax of 440,000 yuan, it recovered slightly. However, compared with previous years, it was only half as much. (3) Bamboo and wood are also one of the province's major export businesses, worth several million yuan annually, with Nanjing and the lower Yangtze River as the sales markets. In recent years, due to the terrible banditry in the production areas, they cannot be transported down the mountains. The Jiangnan group, which operates bamboo and wood businesses, has also seen widespread shutdowns due to traffic obstructions, financial depletion, and blocked remittances. Last year, due to the extremely tight monetary situation and high lending rates, and because those who transported bamboo and wood were often obstructed by bandits on the Gan River, resulting in delays, resulting in losses and bankruptcies were also common. (4) Gan'nan's tungsten ore is also sold to the world. In the past, each dan of tungsten sand could sell for fifty to seventy yuan. Recently, due to the global economic downturn, it only sells for more than ten yuan, and most of the mining areas are bandit-controlled areas. This export is already in dire straits. (5) Ramie cloth has declined sharply due to the impact of linen and bamboo cloth. Crude cloth, which relies on the Korean market, has been phased out since the September 18th Incident. All ramie cloth shops in Fuzhou have gone bankrupt. (6) Tea used to be a major export trade in this province. Green tea was sold to Southeast Asia, Japan, and major ports in the country, and black tea was sold to Russia. In recent years, only a small amount has been sold inside and outside the province, and exports are less than one-tenth of what they used to be. Those who started their business in this field are now in ruins. The above are the main products, and other items are even more depressed. As a result, various special products in this province cannot attract cash, and the social economy is not nourished, and the finance has completely lost its balance, becoming anemia. B. In terms of imports, foreign goods, cloth, cotton yarn, hardware, seafood, sugar, foreign paper, and kerosene are the main items. Among them, in addition to heavy industrial products from Europe and the United States, light industrial products are mostly Japanese goods. Since the vigorous implementation of anti-Japanese goods, Western goods have been more expensive and cannot meet the tastes of those who like cheap goods, and imports have gradually decreased, not as enthusiastic as before. C. Inland commerce is entirely built on the knowledgeable producers and consumers. In other words, it is entirely transferred by the prosperity of local products and the purchasing power of farmers. However, this province has been ravaged by bandits for six years, spreading to sixty counties. Natural disasters and man-made disasters have pressed each other. Local products have been declining day by day, and last year the grain price was only around two yuan, accounting for more than 80% of the province's population. Above all, the farmers have no way to survive and cannot die. How can we talk about consumption and purchasing power? The impact is that all industries are depressed, and business is naturally biological. According to a survey of the market last year, department stores were unsalable, those who operated retail stores were sparsely populated, and those who operated wholesale stores were blocked due to unrest in foreign counties, such as Ganzhou, Ji'an, Hekou, Shangmei, Pingxiang, Jingdezhen, Yuanzhou, and Xiushui. The peddling merchants have disappeared, so even if they use methods such as large price reductions, large sales, buy one get one free, and half-price discounts, they cannot attract customers. Most industries in this city are outwardly strong but inwardly weak, relying entirely on money shops to discount loans for turnover. At this moment, due to the poor market, the number of bankruptcies is increasing, such as Yudechang Money Shop and Tiancheng Fur Shop, etc., with fraudulent activities involving tens of thousands of dollars or more. The first to be affected are the money shops, so that the financial community is wary and dare not release loans. Since the money shops do not dare to release loans, the market feels more crisis-ridden. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce recently saw that the world is getting worse, and many people have gone bankrupt due to business failures, while there are also intentional frauds, obvious bankruptcies, secret escapes, and those who are free from the law. Creditors often have lawsuits for many years against debtors, and there is no solution. For example, Yulong, Meihuanji, Jinchang, and other companies have been bankrupt since last year, and creditors still have no solution to them. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the National Federation of Commerce of Shanghai and the Chambers of Commerce of various provinces and cities, requesting that they unanimously advocate that debt disputes be classified as administrative scope, so as to correct judicial delays and address the prevailing trend of fraud, and maintain the market. That is also out of desperation. (11th)

Laiyang County in Shandong Province During Military Disaster

Losses Reached More Than 5.8 Million Yuan

Jinan Correspondence: During the recent war between Han and Liu, the losses in various counties in Jiaodong were extremely heavy. The provincial government has ordered various counties to investigate the amount of losses for relief purposes. Among them, in Laiyang County, after Liu's troops retreated, the local community organized a post-disaster committee to investigate the losses suffered by the entire county due to the military disaster. It has now been investigated and reported to the county government, and the county government has forwarded it to the provincial government, requesting that it find a way to provide relief, and requesting that the next busy season's land tax and surcharges be exempted, so as to alleviate the people's difficulties. Today (10th), the provincial government's political affairs meeting discussed this case and the case of Laiyang people's request for relief. It was decided to merge it with the disaster relief case of the 199th meeting for review and unified relief. According to the investigation and report of the Laiyang County Post-Disaster Committee, the losses reached more than 5.8 million yuan, including 52 townships, 301 villages, 12,444 households, and 700,373 victims. Losses of 2,276,609 yuan. Due to the incident, farmers abandoned soybean and sweet potato fields that were not harvested, and wheat fields that were not planted, totaling 120,000 mu (a unit of land area), with an average loss of 9 yuan per mu, totaling 1.08 million yuan. In the past, the supplies provided to Liu's troops amounted to 2.03 million yuan. This time, Liu's troops were transferred, requiring 6,000 mules and large carts, at 70 yuan each, totaling 420,000 yuan. The total direct losses of the above amounted to 5,800,6609 yuan. Other indirect losses cannot be calculated. (10th)

Jiaoji Railway Prepares for Combined Water and Land Transportation

Appointed Members of the Preparatory Committee to Formulate Regulations with Eight Amendments

Qingdao Correspondence: In order to expand its business and facilitate transportation, the Jiaoji Railway Bureau recently established a preparatory committee for combined water and land transportation, and promoted Peng Dongyuan, a member of the road, to serve as the director of the committee, responsible for organization and active implementation. The regulations of the preparatory committee have now been drafted, and Commissioner Peng has sent a letter to the Chief Auditor Ye Chongxun, the Chief of General Affairs Qian, the Chief of the Office Song Qiangming, the Chief of Vehicle Affairs Kagamiyama Gaku, the Chief of the Office Tan Shukui, the Chief of the Accounting Office Gao Lun Jin, the Chief of the Office Oishi Sadayoshi, Secretaries Yin Yuanyi and Guo Dazhong, Liang Huanding, the head of the compilation section of the General Affairs Office, Cao Changqi, the head of the transportation section of the Vehicle Affairs Office, Wei Xin, the head of the business section, Ouyang Hong, the head of the general audit section of the Accounting Office, and Liu Dide, the head of the first section of the Vehicle Affairs Office, as members of the committee, and in accordance with the provisions of Article 6 of the committee's regulations, dispatched members Liang Huanding, Guo Dazhong, and also served as the first and second section chiefs of the committee. Other staff members have been dispatched separately by the Road Bureau upon the committee's special request. The address of the committee is temporarily located at 29 Taiping Road, and it has applied to the Management Bureau for the issuance of the official seal of the committee to facilitate progress. The regulations of the preparatory committee are recorded as follows: Article 1. This road is established to expand its business and facilitate transportation, and a preparatory committee for combined water and land transportation is specially established to prepare for all matters related to combined water and land transportation. Article 2. The organization of this committee shall be composed of one member publicly elected by the Management Committee as the Director of the Committee, and senior staff members of various offices — to — individuals shall be members, and two of the members of this committee shall be designated as deputy directors. Article 3 The duties of this committee are as follows: (1) Matters related to investigation and contact of combined water and land transportation; (2) Matters related to the planning and equipment of combined water and land transportation; (3) Matters related to drafting contract drafts. Article 4. Important matters of this committee shall be implemented by the Director of the Committee convening a plenary meeting and resolving them. Ordinary matters shall be handled directly by the Director of the Committee and the Deputy Director of the Committee in consultation. Article 5. The Director of the Committee shall be the chairman of the meeting of this committee. When the Director of the Committee is absent, the Deputy Director of the Committee shall act as his agent in turn. Article 6. The first and second shares shall be set up, each with one section chief and several clerks and recorders, who shall be concurrently filled by the staff members of each office of the Bureau. Article 7. The staff members of this committee shall handle all affairs of this committee under the command of the Director of the Committee. Article 8. These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (January 11th)

This time, the implementation of the new chapter, can the company continue to handle the payment of donations according to the original plan, or will it collect donations and pay them to the Department for allocation? This is the second request for approval. This is the third request for approval. The above three points are all special circumstances in this county. This time, the implementation of the new chapter, how should it be handled? Feng Zhanhai's Representative Appeals to Support Association for Assistance

Tai Feng, the representative of Feng Zhanhai stationed in Shanghai, sent a letter to the Shanghai Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association yesterday, stating, "Respectfully, we recently received a letter from our commander-in-chief, forwarded by our office in Beiping, stating that since our army arrived in Rehe, we have been deeply grateful for the various assistance provided by the patriotic gentlemen in Shanghai. All 40,000 soldiers are filled with admiration. However, since arriving in Kailu, we have been actively replenishing our forces. However, the Japanese bandits have now reinforced their troops and are attacking Yuguan, attempting to seize Rehe. In the smoke and fog, they engaged in hand-to-hand combat. This rare and arduous battle has exhausted our incomplete replenishment supplies. We urgently hope to appeal to the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, the Northeast Refugee Relief Association, the Recover Lost Territories Association, representatives of overseas Chinese, the Women's Relief Association, and various organizations in Shanghai to plead for assistance. At this critical moment, please do not neglect us." Feng was in the army and fought alongside them for a year, witnessing the soldiers' dedication to the country and their disregard for their own lives. After each battle, there were numerous casualties, but the morale of the soldiers did not diminish. They persevered and advanced with unwavering spirit. However, due to insufficient ammunition, they often lost the final push. Recalling the past, Feng feels heartbroken. Feng was sent south this time to appeal to all parties, and our commander-in-chief has already telegraphed your association. Now, based on the previous letter forwarded by the Beiping office, the situation is extremely urgent. We earnestly request your association to provide assistance and allocate funds as soon as possible with a patriotic fervor and send personnel to comfort them in order to encourage the soldiers and strengthen their determination to fight to the death. The reason why Li, Ding, and Ma retreated to the Russian border was due to a lack of economic resources and ammunition. The painful past is unbearable to recall. The Japanese invaders are now planning to use the troops at Yuguan to seize all of Rehe and then attack Beiping and Tianjin. The facts are clear and visible to all. According to the strength of Feng's troops, they occupy the main position in Rehe. If they are allowed to follow the same path as Li, Ding, and Ma and are annihilated without combat power, then Rehe will be lost, and there will be no hope of restoring the Northeast. The demise of the nation is imminent, and the lessons of the past are not far off. The past is terrifying. Please help the association quickly raise material and economic assistance and appeal to all sectors to maintain the unity of Feng's troops and boost the courage of the soldiers. The matter is pressing and cannot be delayed any longer. We express our utmost urgency in this letter."

Muslims to Hold Memorial Service for An Dexin

Elite Soldier Ha Decheng, Who Died for His Country at Yuguan, Expresses His Views

Battalion Commander An Dexin, a Muslim, died for his country in the Battle of Yuguan on the 7th of this month. The soldiers of his entire battalion, who had been influenced by Commander An, also died on the battlefield without a single survivor. After receiving a report from the Muslim church in Beiping, the various Muslim churches in this city expressed their deep sorrow for Commander An's sacrifice for the country and will hold a memorial service. The preparations for the memorial service have already begun. The details are as follows:

Preparing for Memorial Service: After receiving the telegram from fellow Muslims in Beiping on the 9th, informing them of Commander An's death, the Muslim community in this city gathered at the Zhejiang Road Mosque on the 11th to discuss preparations for the memorial service. A preparatory committee was formed, with Da Fushou as the chairman, assisted by various imams. A telegram of condolence was sent to Commander An's family, and all Muslim churches around the world were notified to hold religious memorial services in their respective churches at the same time on a designated date. Replies from various places have been arriving in succession. The date will be decided at the second preparatory meeting, and memorial services will be held separately in various places at the same time.

Light of Islam: Yesterday, Imam Ha Decheng told a Datong News Agency reporter that Commander An was the second Muslim to sacrifice his life for the country. During the Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu, General Zuo Baogui, a Muslim, died in battle, and his deeds are recorded in national history. Now, Commander An has also died under the fire of Japanese invaders. Their loyalty, bravery, and righteousness shine brightly, reflecting each other. This is not only the honor of Zuo and An, but also the supreme glory of our Islam.

Generous Compensation for An: Ha continued, "Currently, members of our community are actively preparing for the memorial service to comfort An's spirit in heaven. Before his death, An was loyal and honest in his official duties, so his family is now in dire straits. Now, various churches are raising funds from members to provide generous compensation to An's family."

The Current Situation of Japanese Goods Dumping in China Amidst Boycott

Japanese Coal Sales in Shanghai Reach Over 90,000 Tons per Month

Japanese Cement Sales Reach Over One Million Barrels Annually

Fisheries Company Launches Large-Scale Aggression

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, noting the sharp increase in Japanese goods imports and their dumping throughout the Yangtze River region, averaging about 50,000 pieces per week, has reiterated the resolution passed by the members' assembly to sever economic ties with Japan and strictly prevent it. A Xinsheng News Agency reporter investigated the goods that Japan is dumping in China, and those that have the deepest impact on domestic goods are listed below:

Coal: Japanese coal dumping is based in Shanghai and Hankou. The policy is to use Fushun coal, transported from the Northeast to Shanghai and Hankou for dumping. Originally, Fushun coal could fetch a net price of 6.50 Japanese yen per ton in Hanyang, and even in Dalian, it could fetch 6.20 yen. However, by shipping it to Shanghai and Hankou, it only fetches a net price of 4.03 Japanese yen. The willingness to forgo heavy profits and the intention to dump are clear. They are also exploiting the weak capital of Chinese merchants by selling coal to small shops on credit. The plan is very meticulous. However, according to a survey by the Kailuan Mining Company, the sales of Kailuan No. 2 fines last year were only ten taels and seven-and-a-half qian [blank space]. However, the stockpiles in various places, including over 600,000 tons in Qinhuangdao, over 130,000 tons in Hankou, and 150,000 tons below Wuhu, totaling one million tons, are all affected by Japanese coal dumping. This is not due to the high cost of transporting domestic coal. The transportation costs for Kailuan and other types of coal, except for a few exceptions such as Shanxi coal, are calculated per ton per kilometer: Kailuan 15 yuan, Zhongxing 5 yuan, Jingxing 6 yuan, and Liuhegou 82 yuan. The transportation costs are quite reasonable. The main reason for the sluggish sales of domestic coal is still Japanese coal dumping. For example, in August of last year, the actual sales of Japanese coal in Shanghai reached 45,831 tons, and Fushun coal reached 45,582 tons, which is a staggering amount.

Cement: Japanese cement dumping targets various coastal ports in China, including Shanghai, Tianjin, Shantou, Xiamen, Qingdao, and Guangzhou. Along the Yangtze River, Hankou is the center. The dumping methods, in addition to price cuts, also involve directly soliciting users, such as construction factories, public works bureaus, and tram companies. The current selling price in Shanghai, including delivery, is about three taels per barrel, compared to only 24 fen in Japan. The selling price of domestic cement in Shanghai is 4.6 taels per barrel, plus consolidated tax and commission, totaling 5.35 taels per barrel, which is more expensive by over 2.3 taels. The annual production of domestic cement is about 3.7 million barrels, and the total sales in various ports across the country is about 2.7 million barrels. The remaining 1 million barrels have been seized by Japanese cement. Originally, domestic cement could be self-sufficient. Even in terms of quality, although it may not be superior to Japanese cement, there is not much difference. Only the dumping of Japanese goods has prevented it from selling well.

Fisheries: Japanese aggression in China's fishing industry began as early as the Meiji 28th year and is based in Qingdao, Shanghai, and Hong Kong. From 1919 to 1921, there were 34 Japanese hand-operated net fishing vessels in Shanghai, and the value of the annual fishing products encroached upon exceeded 800,000 yuan. After the Chinese government implemented fishing vessel taxes, Japanese vessels became even more cunning. After fishing illegally in our territorial waters, they would first transport the catch to Dalian and then ship it to Shanghai via Chinese merchant ships, secretly evading taxes. Last year, the Japan Fisheries Company, with a capital of 30 million yuan, organized a fisheries company in Yingkou and Dalian, launching a large-scale aggression. On June 1st of last year, Japanese fish imports amounted to 1,200 boxes, on the 2nd, 800 boxes, and on November 28th, another 697 boxes were imported, which is truly alarming. After Japanese fish reach our country, they implement a dumping policy. The selling price of fish produced in Ningbo and other places in our country is about 16 or 17 yuan per dan, while Japanese fish are sold at a reduced price of 10 to 12 yuan.

Russian Merchants Active in China

Will Face Off with Japanese Goods

According to business circles, after the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, Russian goods are being shipped to China, with Vladivostok as the starting point for sea routes, importing to Guangzhou, Shanghai, Tianjin, Xiamen, Hankou, and other places. Land routes use Outer Mongolia as the central transportation point, transporting to Suiyuan, Zhangjiakou, and other places in North China. Timber, kerosene, woolen textiles, cotton textiles, and hardware are the main items, posing a potential head-on conflict with Japanese goods. In particular, textiles, woolens, and felt items are sufficient to deal a fatal blow to Japanese goods. The raw materials for Japanese cotton and woolen textiles still largely come from China, while Russia utilizes the latest machinery managed by the government, making the cost of production about one-third of that of Japanese goods. It is reported that Russian goods in the three northeastern provinces are already competing with Japanese merchants. Japanese goods selling for one yuan can be obtained for six jiao from Russia. It is said that the Soviet Union recently instructed its commercial personnel stationed in South China to start signing commercial contracts with major Chinese companies and stores. It is understood that in Shanghai and Hankou, eight companies, including a certain timber company and a certain cotton cloth company, have already signed such contracts with Russian merchants, and the rest are still under negotiation. Since last month, the Soviet Union has successively imported over 20,000 tons of goods, paying customs duties in accordance with customs regulations. It is reported that another 50,000 tons will be arriving in China next month. It is expected that the period of Russian merchants' activity in China will be in March, when there will be a shift in the business sector.

Xue Dubi, member of the Central Committee and member of the National Government, recently resigned from his position as member of the National Government, stating that he will practice law in Shanghai. Now that Yuguan has fallen, the gateway to North China is wide open. Huang Boqiao Talks About the Railway Bureau's Reforms

Increase Third and Fourth Class Cars and Steam Cars, Expand the Visitor Reception System

Since Director Huang Boqiao took office at the Shanghai-Nanjing and Nanjing-Shanghai Railway Administration, he has made many efforts to rectify everything internally. A Xinsheng News Agency reporter visited the director yesterday afternoon. Huang said that since he took over, there have not been many changes in the internal staff. Only the Ministry of Railways has cut the redundant positions of commissioners, and he has dismissed 15 people. In addition, he has reassigned two secretaries. The remaining specialized personnel who have served for many years [character unclear] have not

moved, to warm hands. As for the rumors of changes, it is likely a misunderstanding of the aforementioned dismissals. Zheng Baozhao, the director of the Traffic Department, is an expert and will definitely not be changed, so that we can jointly take responsibility for rectification. In addition, the Railway Administration has now decided to implement the following two reforms: 1. Increase the number of third and fourth class cars on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway and the number of steam cars on the Shanghai-Songjiang Railway by one train each to improve the crowded and uncomfortable conditions of the third and fourth class passenger cars in the past, while striving to pay attention to the cleanliness and hygiene of the cars to reassure passengers. 2. Expand the existing visitor reception system. The existing visitor reception system has only been available for important central figures, and the scope is too narrow. In the future, all visitor reception personnel will be required to wear uniforms and badges for identification, providing guidance on railway transportation and consultation for passengers from other places to facilitate merchants. In addition, the current scattered office locations in the bureau will be moved to a centralized location to facilitate public business. The Railway Administration staff had previously requested a year-end bonus. After he repeatedly explained the economic situation of the bureau and made the income and expenditure accounts public, the staff understood. Therefore, the strike issue has now been completely resolved.

In addition, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Nanjing-Shanghai Railway Administration sent a letter to this newspaper stating, "Dear Sir, we have read the news item 'Large-Scale Dismissals of Redundant Personnel in the Railway Bureau' in your newspaper, which is largely inconsistent with the facts. Most of the senior officials in the various departments of our bureau are specialized personnel and have served in the railway for many years with considerable history. Except for Sun Xuexiu, the new director of the Materials Department appointed by the Ministry of Railways, the remaining senior officials have not been changed. The personnel dismissed this time are those who were nominally employed but did not report for duty or were not loyal to their duties. The reports in today's newspapers are not accurate. We are afraid that the rumors will be confused, so we are writing to you to request that you investigate and correct the record."

The Preparatory Committee for the Chicago Exposition Will Hold an Exhibition of Collected Items

The Opening Ceremony Will Be Held on February 1st at the Academia Sinica

The Preparatory Committee for the Chicago Exposition previously sent letters to various provinces and cities requesting them to collect products locally for the upcoming Chicago Expo. A large number of products have now been collected from various places. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency interviewed He Bingxian, the Director of the International Trade Bureau, yesterday. According to him, the preparatory committee has decided to hold an opening ceremony for the exhibition of collected items at the Academia Sinica, across from Zhaofeng Park in Shanghai West, on February 1st. All members and manufacturers from various places will participate at that time. It is reported that Chen Gongbo, the Minister of Industry, may personally come to Shanghai on the opening day.

China National Aviation Corporation's Bengbu Aircraft Took Off from Haizhou Yesterday

It Will Pass Qingdao at Noon and Arrive in Beiping Today

China National Aviation Corporation's Bengbu aircraft, which flies the Shanghai-Beiping route, departed from Shanghai the day before yesterday. However, due to poor weather conditions en route, it was inconvenient to fly and landed at Haizhou Airport. It took off from Haizhou again yesterday morning and arrived in Qingdao at 12:10 PM. The journey was smooth. The aircraft is scheduled to fly directly from Qingdao to Beiping this morning. If the weather is suitable en route, it will reach its destination at noon today.

In addition to the deduction by the Postal Administration of the Directorate General of Posts and the Accounting Office of the Supply Division, this notice is hereby issued for your information."

The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Instructs Companies to Register According to Law

Must Complete Registration Before June 30th, Otherwise Penalties Will Be Imposed According to Law

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to various trade associations yesterday, relaying the instruction No. 7365 from the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs: "The Ministry of Industry's instruction No. 15461 states that Article 18 of the General Rules for Merchants stipulates that businesses should not use the word "company" or similar words in their names unless they operate in accordance with company regulations. This also applies to those who inherit the business of a company but do not continue to operate it in accordance with company regulations. Furthermore, a company may not be established until it has been registered with the competent authorities in the location of its headquarters. Article 114 of the same law states that a company may not issue shares until it has been registered. Article 231, Section 1 and Section 6 of the same law stipulate penalties for those who fail to apply for registration according to law or who illegally issue shares. Therefore, a company may not be established and may not issue shares unless it is organized and registered according to law. Recently, it has been found that some merchants in various provinces and cities are operating businesses or are not organized as companies but are falsely using the name of a company, or are organized as a company but have not applied for registration. They should be banned according to law. Furthermore, companies that have not been registered as legal entities have not obtained qualifications, and their types of organization have not been determined. They often claim to be limited liability companies, but because they have not been registered, they must bear unlimited liability to the outside world. It is clear that they started operating before they were registered, and because they have not been registered, they cannot prevent others from imitating their brands. The company itself suffers greatly. The responsibilities of directors and supervisors are even more important. If the registration is delayed due to unclear procedures or inconvenient transportation, it may be excusable in terms of sentiment, but it is still not in accordance with the law. Therefore, it is hereby reiterated that all companies established in the future should apply for registration within the time limit stipulated in Article 5 of the Company Law. Companies that have already been established but have not yet applied for registration must apply for registration in accordance with the law before June 30th, 1933. If they fail to comply by the deadline, they will be punished according to law once they are discovered. Furthermore, Article 31 of the Implementing Rules of the Company Law stipulates that the registration certificate of a company shall be issued by the Ministry of Industry after registration. Article 5 of the Company Registration Rules stipulates that company registration is only confirmed after the Ministry of Industry issues a license. Therefore, in terms of procedure, the registration of a company must be finally approved and licensed by the Ministry before it can be considered confirmed and have legal effect. In addition to distributing and publishing a notice in the newspaper, the bureau is hereby ordered to provide practical guidance and strictly inspect and, after receiving the order, immediately issue a public notice so that all companies will apply to the bureau for registration and transfer to the Ministry for registration within the specified time limit to avoid penalties and respect the law. Be sure to comply with this order."

The County Government Finds It Difficult to Raise Funds for Relief Bonds for the War Zone

The Shanghai County Government previously received instructions from the province and county to raise Jiangsu relief bonds for the war zone. The Director of the Finance Bureau, Wang, went to the province to collect the bonds. Because the war zone needs funds urgently, in addition to the provincial departments urging collection, Commissioner Li Yi was sent to the county government the day before yesterday to supervise and urge collection. After meeting with County Magistrate Yan, it was found that the county has become a poor area since it was divided with the municipal government. In addition, it was affected by last year's Shanghai battle, so people's livelihoods are declining. Most farmers are self-cultivating their own fields and there are no large landowners. Now is the time to collect the winter tax, so even if they solicit donations, it would be in vain. Therefore, after consulting with the provincial commissioner, Yan decided to wait until the winter tax collection is over before the Finance Bureau makes efforts to solicit donations. The commissioner has already returned to the province to report.

Achievements of the Jinpu Railway in Responsible Transportation Last Month

丨In fact, the revenue increased by more than 470,000 yuan compared with the same month of the previous year丨

News from the transportation industry: the railway is responsible for transportation, and the first to prepare for implementation is the Jinpu Railway. The stations south of Xuzhou on the railway began to implement it on September 1st of last year. On November 1st, all stations, large and small, north and south of the railway, implemented responsible transportation for both carload and less-than-carload shipments. The monthly freight revenue settlement was compared with the revenue of the same month of the previous year, and it was found that the revenue had increased by more than 542,000 yuan, which has been reported in the newspaper and has been highly valued by the authorities.

The preliminary results have now been settled. The settlement for the first ten days of the month shows an increase of 114,654.80 yuan compared with the revenue for the same month of the previous year, an increase of 275,846.73 yuan for the middle ten days, and a decrease of 165,470.07 yuan for the last ten days. Therefore, the final freight revenue for the month increased by only 225,030.09 yuan compared with the revenue for the same month of the previous year. At first glance, it seems to be less than the previous month, but the end of December is the time for year-end settlement and collection. As a result, the revenue on the books is only this amount. Furthermore, the various armies along the railway were very busy with troop deployments during that month, and the transportation of military rations and equipment totaled more than 100 military trains. This is also a major reason for the decrease in freight transportation. Without the above two conditions, plus the estimated business volume of more than 84,000 yuan in the last ten days, the actual increase in freight revenue compared with the same month of the previous year would be more than 473,500 yuan.

Repercussions of the Shazhou Land Price Limit Compensation

Business owners Lu Fenghan and others oppose the illegal disposition of the Shangbao Shazhou Official Property Bureau. Yesterday, they submitted a document to the mayor, stating, "Regarding the Shangbao Shazhou Official Property Bureau causing hardship to the people and dereliction of duty through illegal disposition, we earnestly request your review and approval and swift consultation with the Jiangsu Provincial Government's Department of Finance to order a halt to these actions, in order to prevent disturbances and maintain property rights. We, the petitioners, in accordance with the Ministry regulations in the twelfth year of the Republic, registered for and received the Shazhou land in the twenty-seventh section of Gaoqiao, totaling 62.5 mu each for Ziyun and Songmei, and 37.5 mu each for Jiansun and Mingjia, bearing grain taxes and fulfilling obligations for many years. The procedures were complete, and we lived in peace for a long time. Unexpectedly, last winter, we suddenly received an order from the Shangbao Shazhou Official Property Bureau, setting a deadline to pay the land price compensation. Subsequently, they forcibly halved the disposition. We, the petitioners, were extremely shocked upon hearing this. Considering the matter to be bizarre and unclear, we went to the bureau to inquire about the details, asking about the legal basis and the reasons for this action. Unexpectedly, the bureau acted arrogantly and arbitrarily, claiming that if we were asked to pay, we should just pay, and there was no need to discuss any reasons. In this situation, we, the petitioners, were at a loss, unsure of what to do. Just as we were about to file for relief, we received a notice from your office's Land Bureau, stating that the Shangbao Shazhou Official Property Bureau's official letter mentioned that Lu Ziyun and others originally received more than 190 mu of beach land in the twenty-seventh section, and due to unpaid land prices, a halved disposition was to be made. It requested that the four beach land certificates of the said landholders be sent over for verification, in order to issue certificates for half of the land. Upon receiving this notice, we checked the case. It concerns the integrity of the land under your jurisdiction and has already been reviewed and rejected by the Land Bureau. We dare to present to your Excellency the complete procedures for registering for the Shazhou land in accordance with the Ministry's regulations, as well as the bureau's illegal disposition, in detail: 1. Article 10 of the 'Regulations for the Clearance of Jiangsu Shazhou Land' promulgated by the Ministry stipulates that the value of Shazhou land is divided into two categories: 1. Land that has already been enclosed and cultivated: (a) Top-grade Shazhou land: 10 yuan per mu; (b) Medium-grade Shazhou land: 8 yuan per mu; (c) Lower-grade Shazhou land: 6 yuan per mu. All of the above must be paid in full at once. 2. Land that has not yet been enclosed and cultivated: (a) Top-grade grassy beach: 5 yuan per mu; (b) Medium-grade grassy beach: 4 yuan per mu; (c) Lower-grade grassy beach: 3 yuan per mu. After future enclosure and cultivation, the original price will still be charged in full at once. Those who have already paid 5 yuan will pay another 5 yuan, those who have already paid 4 yuan will pay another 4 yuan, and those who have already paid 3 yuan will pay another 3 yuan. The total amount paid in two installments will be the same as the amount paid for cultivated land, and no further price will be collected thereafter. The Shazhou land paid by us, the petitioners, was in accordance with the third item of the first category of the said article, paying 6 yuan per mu for lower-grade Shazhou land in one lump sum. There is no need to pay any additional compensation, which is very clear. According to the law, there is no obligation to pay any additional compensation. Now, the bureau is arbitrarily and recklessly extorting money and forcibly imposing a halved disposition, which is a disregard for the Ministry's regulations and the credibility of the nation, and is absurd and illegal. It is difficult to remain silent. This is our first request to forward this to the Ministry to order a halt to these actions. 2. Even if we take a step back and consider that there may be changes to the aforementioned regulations after the price was paid in accordance with the Ministry's promulgated regulations, according to the legal principle that laws should not be applied retroactively, these changes cannot have any binding effect on us, the petitioners, especially if the legal regulations have never been changed. If the Ministry's regulations stipulate that no further payment is required, but the bureau suddenly orders additional payment and forcibly imposes a halved disposition under the pretext of adjusting the bureau's accounts, treating the people as meat on a chopping board and using Shazhou land as a tool for fraud, it is no different from guiding the people to play with the law. The nation's credibility is completely trampled upon by the bureau, and the people suffer endlessly. The impact will be that people

will not dare to inquire about Shazhou official property, hindering the nation's Shazhou land revenue significantly. This is our second request to forward this to the Ministry to order a halt to these actions. 3. The Shazhou land registered by us, the petitioners, has all been enclosed as lower-grade Shazhou land. We immediately requested the Baoshan County Government to conduct a survey and measurement, completing the procedures. Furthermore, on March 2, 1928, in accordance with the Shazhou Land Clearance Bureau's announcement, we submitted four copies of the Ministry's certificates and four sets of registration documents to the bureau for verification. The bureau verified that the land price had been paid in full in accordance with the Ministry's regulations, and stamped the Ministry's certificates with the Shazhou Land Clearance Bureau's registration seal, marking them with the words "Registered in the Ri (Day) character Shazhou Land Book." We also submitted to your office's Land Bureau an announcement, submitting all the evidence and requesting the issuance of land certificates. The procedures were complete, and the property rights are certain. Now, the Shangbao Shazhou Official Property Bureau, without asking whether the land price has been paid in full or verifying the case files, rashly orders additional payment and illegally imposes a disposition, which is a disregard for the Ministry's regulations and an abuse of power. This is our third request to forward this to the Ministry to order a halt to these actions. 4. Gaoqiao is located in the Shanghai city area and should be under the jurisdiction of your office's Land Bureau according to the law. Others should not overstep their bounds. The integrity of the land is especially a plan already established by your office's Land Bureau. Therefore, those Shazhou official properties that have not yet had their grain taxes increased are given a deadline to pay 40% of the increased assessment fee for cultivated land. Those that have already had their grain taxes increased are notified to exchange their land certificates to secure their property rights. This has been followed consistently, and the people are happy to comply. Now, the Shangbao Shazhou Official Property Bureau is not handling matters in accordance with the law, but is abusing its power to extort money. It seems that the 40% cultivated land compensation fee stipulated by your office's Land Bureau for those that have not yet had their grain taxes increased is met with suspicion and hesitation, hindering its implementation. This not only oppresses the common people but also hinders the integrity of the land under your jurisdiction. This is our fourth request to forward this to the Ministry to order a halt to these actions. Based on the above reasons, according to administrative procedures, we should submit this to the Jiangsu Provincial Government's Department of Finance to order a halt to these actions. However, we fear that the Department of Finance may be deceived by the bureau, making it difficult to achieve the desired effect. Furthermore, Gaoqiao is under your jurisdiction, and if the bureau is allowed to act arbitrarily, it will have a significant impact on the integrity of the land. Therefore, we request your review and swift consultation for the sake of benefit and convenience. Respectfully submitted to Wu, the Mayor of Shanghai City, by petitioners Lu Ziyun, son Fenghan, Fengbo, Lu Meisong, Jian, and Sun Mingjia."

Road Construction Association Advocates for Automobile Consumer Cooperative

Preparations will begin after approval by the Executive Committee soon

Many Fujian and Guangdong business tycoons and overseas Chinese are willing to invest

The China National Road Construction Association, in order to prevent the monopoly and exploitation of automobile consumption and to gradually reduce waste, plans to jointly establish an automobile consumer cooperative with various long-distance automobile companies in the country and all or some automobile owners. This cooperative will specialize in collecting statistics on the quantity and types of automobiles and their required items nationwide, and will negotiate with manufacturers at home and abroad for the lowest wholesale prices, with the aim of achieving transparency, fairness, quality, and affordability. It will also encourage domestic factories to imitate the production of various automobile parts needed, and all users will give priority to purchasing from them, in order to promote production and reclaim profit rights. Currently, the association is drafting the "China Automobile Consumer Cooperative" proposal, which will be submitted to the Executive Committee for approval soon. Afterwards, it will notify all directors to begin preparations and actively implement the plan. It is reported that many Fujian and Guangdong business tycoons and overseas Chinese support the plan and are willing to invest in the establishment of this enterprise. Long-distance automobile companies and highway bureaus in various provinces are particularly hoping that this will become a reality soon, in order to avoid the various difficulties in purchasing parts and the resulting losses.

Screening of the National Goods Movement Parade Film

Initiated by the Shanghai Local Association and others

Filmed by the Morning News' specially contracted Star Film Company

The National Goods Movement Automobile Parade, jointly initiated by the Shanghai Local Association, the China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association, the Mechanical National Goods Factory Federation, and others, was held on New Year's Day this year. Major national goods factories in Shanghai participated enthusiastically. On that day, the automobiles in the parade were of all shapes and colors, competing for beauty and novelty, and all were uniquely designed, truly setting a new unprecedented record for national goods parades. At that time, the Morning News specially contracted the Star Film Company to follow and film the entire event. This film, along with "Adventures on the Battlefield," will be screened alternately at major theaters such as the Central and New Central starting today. Currently, the Morning News is working hand in hand with the national goods industry to continue filming the organization and work of major national goods factories across the country. In the future, these films will be merged and distributed to major theaters nationwide and in Southeast Asia for public screening, widely circulating the film, with the aim of giving the public a deep understanding of national goods during the "National Goods Year."

Snowflakes danced all day yesterday

The Severe Cold in the North, the Righteous Army Fights the Enemy, People in Shanghai Should Also Feel Sympathy

Since the evening of the 11th in this city, it has been snowing for two days without stopping. However, the snow is not very heavy, and the accumulation on the roofs is only about an inch. As for the roads, carts are running horizontally and vertically, and people are coming and going. The snow melts as it falls, only feeling it is hard and slippery, making it difficult to stand. Yesterday morning, the snow was heavier, with goose feather-like flakes fluttering in the wind. At other times, it was like salt scattered from the sky, with snowflakes dancing in competition. Since the two days of snowfall in Shanghai, the bustling city has suddenly turned into a silver world, covered in powder and jade, with a different kind of scenery. At this time, the severe cold in the north, the righteous army fights the enemy, living in a world of ice and snow every day. The people of Shanghai, accustomed to urban life, should also be moved by this, right? Yesterday's temperature was lower than the previous two days. There were cases of poor people freezing to death in the alleys. Moreover, the supply of vegetables in the various vegetable markets was quite scarce, and the prices also increased accordingly. The situation yesterday is recorded below:

Frozen to Death Paupers: Continuous auspicious snow has been falling for three days without stopping, and the temperature has dropped to zero. Therefore, poor people rushing on the roads often freeze to death due to their low resistance. The night before last, a male corpse was found collapsed on the ground in the south of Sanguantang, Tangqiao, Pudong. He was about forty years old, wearing a black cotton jacket and trousers, and a peaked cap. No family members reported the case. The local security officer Zhu Zhangsheng reported to the local court for inspection. In addition, an unidentified man was also found collapsed in a pit latrine in Yu's Family Temple, Pudong. He was about fifty years old, wearing a black cotton jacket, a blue cloth shirt, and single trousers, with black leggings as a skirt and bare feet. There were no family members. The local security officer Yang Baobao reported for investigation. Chief Prosecutor Yang et al. went to verify and confirmed it was death by freezing. They instructed the hall to collect the bodies for burial.

Vegetable Prices Rise: Yesterday, in various small vegetable markets in the city, except for meat which was sold as usual, the fish and shrimp were all frozen. The vendors considered them rare goods and doubled the prices. However, due to the inability of returning hometown vendors and farmers to quickly transport vegetables to Shanghai, the prices of various vegetables rose sharply.

Rickshaw Pullers' Misery: Yesterday, the business of stores along various roads in the city was relatively slow compared to the past. Due to the wind and snow, there were few pedestrians. The rickshaw pullers on the road were shivering, extremely miserable. Most passengers took trams to avoid the wind and snow.

A Short-Sighted Policeman Inspects a Gun Barrel, A Bullet Misfires and Kills Him

Mei Chunzhi, a policeman from the First District Police Station of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, was twenty-six years old and from Tiantai County, Zhejiang Province. After finishing his shift at four o'clock in the afternoon the day before yesterday, he was cleaning his pistol after returning to the station in the morning. Unexpectedly, there was a bullet inside, which he forgot to remove. Because Mei was short-sighted in one eye, he looked into the barrel, and the bullet misfired, hitting Mei's forehead, penetrating his brain, and causing him to fall to the ground. Blood and brains mixed together. The district chief learned of this and immediately sent him to Shanghai Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died that night. Yesterday, the district ordered Lu Rongde, the head of the Sixteen Puling, to report to the local court for inspection. In the afternoon, Chief Prosecutor Yang et al. arrived at the court, verified that it was death by gunshot wound, and the family members collected the body for burial pending verification.

The Wusong Ship Tea Attendants Are Employed by the Company

Regarding the Wusong ship tea attendants, the manager of Taikoo Company told people that in the past, passengers were often treated poorly by the tea attendants and were very dissatisfied. They had repeatedly reported to the company that these tea attendants were not directly employed by the company and did not receive wages. They could only demand tips to make a living. In view of this, the company, in order to ensure the peace of mind of travelers, specially employed the Wusong ship tea attendants themselves, gave them good salaries, and entrusted them with maintaining order, so that they would not make excessive demands on passengers. The company did not sign a contract with any party to retain the tea attendants on each ship.

Pushan Villa's Report on Charitable Deeds in the 21st Year

Pushan Villa has been handling the burial of the exposed remains for years, which is of great importance to public health. Since the Shanghai Incident, it has buried the fallen soldiers and victims in the war zones of Jiangwan and Dachang, which is especially numerous. According to statistics, the total number of coffins buried throughout the year is no less than 36,000, which is a record number of burials in the history of the villa. The number of deaths is extremely tragic. The villa's report on the annual charitable deeds is detailed below: (1) Burial Section: Zhabei Villa buried 1,359 large coffins and 15,068 small coffins from Zhabei, Jiangwan, and the war zone. The Public Concession Public Works Department sent notices to bury unclaimed bodies within the concession, totaling 1,170 large coffins and 11,563 small coffins. Xieqiao Branch buried 44 large coffins and 6,507 small coffins from the French Concession and the South City. Various hospitals of the Chinese Red Cross received 177 large coffins and 16 small coffins. Tongren, Baolong, Renji, and various military hospitals received 72 large coffins and 9 small coffins. The Chinese Jisheng Society received 13 large coffins and 51 small coffins. The Red Swastika Society received 1 large coffin and 19 small coffins. The Shanghai Citizen Local Maintenance Association received 30 large coffins and 2 small coffins. The Shanghai War Zone Refugee Temporary Relief Association received 112 large coffins and 270 small coffins. The Xinwei Relief Association received 8 large coffins and 4 small coffins. The Shanghai Municipal Epidemic Hospital received 76 large coffins and 5 small coffins. Various refugee camps received 24 large coffins and 102 small coffins. In total, 3,088 large coffins and 33,616 small coffins were buried. 15,744 large and small coffins were donated. All the above coffins have been transported to the burial trenches in Zhabei and Nanshi Rihuigang and marked for later collection for burial. (2) Medical Treatment Section: The Baishizi Pushan Hospital on Xinmin Road, Zhabei, provided medicines and gave out money for the year, totaling 41,487 visits. The achievements of the charitable deeds of the villa are great, and the required expenses must also be considerable. It is hoped that philanthropists from all walks of life will cooperate to maintain it and provide assistance continuously, so that it can last forever. Its merits are boundless.

A Tragedy Occurs in the Kitchen of Nanyang Model Middle School

| The Cook Died a Tragic Death |

Chen Genfu, the cook of the private Model Middle School in Shanghai Jiaotong University on Haige Road in West Shanghai, has been contracting the school's meals since 1926, employing twelve people. He lived outside the school at No. 3 Hujiazhai. In the evening, the kitchen affairs were handled by Tao Shengbao (over thirty years old), a fellow villager who specialized in chopping, Chen Jinyong's younger brothers and Tao's introducer Gao Jingwu, who lived together in the school kitchen for three years. Tao Shengbao was honest, had no hobbies, and was trusted by Chen Genfu, the head cook. Unexpectedly, at about 4:00 a.m. yesterday, Chen Caiyun went to the stove in the kitchen with a candle to prepare to cook rice porridge. He suddenly saw Tao Shengbao's body lying horizontally on a pile of wood chips at the stove door. His chest was exposed, his abdomen was bloody, his large intestine was dragged out, and there was blood on the knife wound on his throat. A kitchen knife was left next to the deceased's right knee, and the lower body trousers were pulled down, with the belt untied. Chen immediately reported the situation to Song Baoqing, the police captain of Jiaotong University, who reported it to the Second Sub-Bureau of the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. The patrolman Shi Jintian was dispatched to investigate the school's kitchen and took Gao Jingwu and the other two roommates to the bureau for questioning. He also reported to the General Bureau and ordered the local security officer to report to the court for inspection.

Two Robberies in the Snow

| Liang Lintu Injured While Catching Thieves |

Liang Lintu (26 years old), a Zhejiang native residing at No. 111 Parker Road, went to visit his aunt at No. 295 Shunxing Lane, Republic Road, in the French Concession at about 10:00 a.m. yesterday. As soon as he sat down, four robbers rushed up from downstairs. One robber held a gun and stood guard at the staircase entrance, while three robbers entered the room to search and rob. Liang realized that he had encountered robbers and stepped forward to grab one robber. He shouted for help. The robber was anxious and raised his gun to fire a shot into Liang's left hand. The bullet passed through the palm of his hand. At the same time, the police siren sounded on the road, and nearby detectives gathered and captured two robbers on the spot. The injured Liang Lintu was sent to Renji Police Hospital for treatment by the police station.

A Rickshaw Puller, Heavily in Debt from Gambling on Flower Associations, Hangs Himself

Lu Guanglin, a rickshaw puller from Dongtai, residing at No. 3 Yongji Lane, Wangzhi Road, in the French Concession, was twenty-four years old. He usually had a strong passion for gambling on flower associations, so that his daily work outside was not enough to supply gambling capital. He borrowed money from people to pay for gambling expenses. Recently, due to heavy debts, the end of the lunar year was approaching. Creditors pressed him from all sides. Lu could not cope and suddenly had a short-sighted idea. The night before last, he secretly took a rope from his home and went to the Yongji Lane entrance on Sapo Sai Road, where he hanged himself on the iron gate. At 6:00 a.m. yesterday, Tao Delin, the gatekeeper of the alley, caught sight of him and rushed to rescue him, but he had already died. The corpse was cold and could not be taken down. The car entered the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for corpse examination. He also summoned the deceased's cousin, Lu Guangdu, to the case. That morning at 10:00 a.m., he reported to the Second Special District Court, which appointed Prosecutor Deng to come to the office to verify that the deceased had indeed died by hanging. The corpse was ordered to be collected for burial by the family members after they had signed a guarantee.

Zhong Tianduo, a student of Datong University High School, lived in this city and was only seventeen years old. He was naturally upright. Because of the emergency of the Northeast war and the loss of Yuguan, he was motivated by righteous indignation and could not bear to sit by and watch the country sink, so he had the intention to join the army. On the 10th of this month, he borrowed a uniform and several silver dollars from his classmate Zhang Jun, on the pretext of going to Yiru Photo Studio to take pictures. He has been gone for several days and has not returned to school. His family also did not know where he had gone. On the morning of the 13th, they received a letter from him from Zhenjiang (to Zhang Jun), saying that he had boarded a ship to the north.

Record of Interrogation of Kidnappers in the Sun Yangru Case

Kidnappers Each Had Specific Responsibilities

Confessions Involved Mutual Blame

Sun Yangru, a native of Anhui, 47 years old, was the manager of Tongfeng Company at No. 5 Nianji Road. At 4 p.m. on the 14th of last month, Sun drove his own car, No. 2648, to No. 67 Xieqiao Road to visit a friend. When the car passed the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Xieqiao Road, it was suddenly blocked by three kidnappers. Each held a pistol and jumped into the car. Two of the kidnappers, armed with guns, watched over Sun, while the third kidnapper drove the car in Sun's place, heading straight to Fuli Road, Avenue Petain, in the French Concession. There, they switched to another car, No. 6335, which the kidnappers had pre-parked at the location, and drove to No. 5 Yideli, Raoul Road, where they hid Sun. They then sent a letter to Sun's family, demanding a huge ransom. Sun's family, fearing harm to Sun, concealed the matter from the police. It was not until the morning of the 27th that Lu Liankui, Chief Inspector of the Detective Division of the Central Police Station, learned that some bandits were hiding in Room 414 of the East Asia Hotel on Nanjing Road. He immediately led Chinese detectives Liu Shaokui, Feng Zhiming, Shao Jingfan, and Dong Zhaobin to the hotel and arrested Huang Jingtang. Subsequently, in Room 343 of the Huizhong Hotel, Yang Baofu, Tang Jinsheng (aka Xu Hairong), Ma Lisan, Gao Shanqing, and others were arrested. They confessed to being involved in the Sun case and revealed the location where Sun was being held. Lu then led Chinese detectives Zhou Honglin, Wang Guilin, Shen Tianbao, Xie Futang, Bao Lisheng, and other Chinese and foreign detectives to Raoul Road, where they safely rescued Sun Yangru. At the time, there was a struggle with the bandits, resulting in two bandits, Lu Ge and Wang Yaohua, being injured. Lu later died from his injuries. Two pistols and more than thirty rounds of ammunition were seized. Arrests of accomplices continued, resulting in the capture of a total of twenty-two male and female bandits. A car, No. 6335, used in the kidnapping, and Huang Jingtang's car, No. 11624, were seized. The case was handed over to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention. After investigation, seven people, including Wang Ziang, were found to be innocent and released. The remaining fifteen, including Yang Baofu, Tang Jinsheng, Ma Lisan, Gao Shanqing, Wang Weichuan, Wu Anwen, Wang Yaohua, Guo Yusheng, Wang Chunshan, Jia Jingshan, Huang Jingtang, Li Xitang, Chen Jushuo, Wu Wangshi, and Wang Dingshi, were identified as follows: Yang Baofu and Huang Jingtang were the leaders of the case; Tang Jinsheng and Ma Lisan were responsible for hiding Sun; Gao Shanqing purchased the car; Wu Anwen drove the car; Wang Yaohua carried out the kidnapping; Guo Yusheng and Wang Chunshan were responsible for guarding Sun; Jia Jingshan was in charge of contact; Wang Weichuan was the gatekeeper; and the others were accomplices in the case. Yesterday afternoon, Qian Hongtang, Presiding Judge of the Criminal Division of the First Special Court, continued the trial in the first criminal court. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, explained the circumstances of the case and stated that two seals with Ma Lisan's alias, Yuan Jinxiang, were found in the bandit's lair. After Sun was kidnapped, a diary was taken by the bandits, with the English phrase "Please remember December 14th" written in it. All the seized items were presented to the court. When questioned, Tang Jinsheng and Yang Baofu confessed that they, Wang Yaohua, and others had discussed the kidnapping at the East Asia Hotel. Later, Yang obtained 100 yuan from Huang Jingtang, and Xue Dexing (who is at large) rented a house. Ma Lisan, Guo Yusheng, Lu Ge, and Wang Weichuan lived inside. Car No. 6335 was purchased by Gao Shanqing for 800 yuan. Wang Weichuan confessed to being responsible for cooking and buying food. Wu Wangshi confessed that she was hired by Xue as a servant and was not allowed to go upstairs, so she knew nothing about the kidnapping. Wu Anwen confessed that Xue asked him to drive car No. 6335 and on December 14th, ordered him to pick up a guest on Fuli Road, but he did not know it was a kidnapping. Guo Yusheng confessed that Tang Jinsheng asked him to guard Sun, and he guarded him for more than ten days. Huang Jingtang confessed that when Wen Yingxing was the head of the Public Safety Bureau, he served as the captain of the police force and handled many major cases, which made him hated by bandits, so he is now being falsely accused and did not participate in the case. Chen Jushuo confessed that he founded a charitable organization in Jiangdu and is currently the director of the Jiangdu Poor Children's Home, earning 3,000 yuan a year. He asked why he would commit such a criminal act. The other defendants gave evasive confessions. Chen Jushuo and others hired lawyers E Sen and Fan Gang to defend them. Judge Qian reviewed the confessions and, as the case still required investigation, adjourned the trial for one week. Li Xitang was released on bail of 1,000 yuan. Wu Wangshi and Wang Dingshi were released on bail to be available for questioning at any time.

Reader's Forum

Let's All "Do"

丨Letter from Mu Jun丨

I read the letter from Zhang Yuanjun in the January 10th issue of this column, and I felt immensely refreshed by his discussion of the questions raised by Gao Mianzhi (Why is education not doing well? Why don't farmers have enough to eat?), like chewing a snow pear! It's so much better than vaguely talking about "the whole social problem." Alas! Millions upon millions of oppressed people only know how to "endure hardship," even more than cattle and horses, eating "tree bark and grass roots" until they die! "Inexplicable"! This is how the masses live, and this is how the status quo is sustained! But will it last? It looks like it's about to collapse! Zhang Jun said: "Now we can only clench our fists and stand up and do!" Really, now we should all stand up and "do" this "collapse"! Friends! Let's all "do"!

Which Way Should We Go?

丨Letter from Qian Xingnong丨

Reading this column these days, we can hear many painful cries erupting from under heavy oppression. These cries are truly from the masses! We believe that as long as someone is a youth of the times, they should know what changes their current society will undergo. Unexpectedly, in the December 30th issue of this column, I found a letter from Zhang Conglong, who advocated that this column should publish more letters about studying natural science and starting businesses to solicit like-minded people, and should not just let unemployed people complain and heartbroken people show off. I really don't know if he is talking in his sleep or awake! Originally, what we have here is a bloody atmosphere. A rich young master jumping out of a car must find it annoying to hear beggars begging for food. Zhang finds this column "tasteless," which is exactly the same! It's just a pity that Zhang's footing is not very stable. Look, he's about to fall! At that time, we'll see if Zhang wants to make any "complaints" or shout a few "slogans"! Here, which way should we go? Wake up, Zhang! Otherwise, we can only watch you follow the old decline and decline quickly!

Editor's Note: Regarding the errors in Zhang Conglong's letter, we have already made some corrections in our previous reply (see December 30th issue). Now we have received another letter from Qian, which, although it does not contain any new insights, is still worth referencing, so we have recorded and published it here.

True "Charity"

丨Letter from a Drifter丨

Reading the letter from Ms. Zhao Jinglan (Poor Family and Heavy Burden) published in the December 29th issue of this column, we are filled with infinite emotion.

I feel that Zhao's family is in an extremely dangerous situation. Anyone with a bit of passion should express sympathy after reading her letter.

Being a person, especially in our Chinese society, whether as an individual or a family, if you don't plan ahead and be careful every step of the way, when you encounter a situation where you have nowhere to turn for help, society will absolutely not forgive or help you. It's already extremely lucky if they don't say you're "suffering the consequences of your own actions."

I always believe that people should help each other, but what kind of world is this now? If you want to find a truly enthusiastic charitable person who specializes in helping those with nowhere to turn for help, I'm afraid you can't find one in ten thousand people.

I also come from a difficult and impoverished background, so I am always willing to help those in need as much as I can. Unfortunately, my power is too weak and my financial resources are too limited. Otherwise, I would really be willing to help Zhao, and I sincerely hope that like-minded comrades can unite and come up with a way to help them so that her family can continue to survive. This is a great deed, and saving people is also saving oneself. Cultivating talents for the country is also an act of patriotism. Finally, I can only comfort Ms. Zhao with the saying "Heaven never bars all roads".

Reply: The letter expresses deep sympathy for the suffering of Zhao's family and a willingness to "help others in need" with personal strength, and further hopes that everyone can unite to help Zhao. Such concern shows the kindness of your heart, which fills us with infinite respect! However, there is one point that you should pay attention to: Will our temporary help to Zhao enable her to escape her bitter situation forever? Even if it can, there are countless others like Zhao in today's society, and many are about to starve to death. According to your relief method, can we help them all escape their bitter situation one by one? Of course not. Then, we can only save Zhao alone, what about the others? Therefore, the current problem cannot be solved by "charity". We must change the way things are so that everyone can be saved. This is an ironclad fact! Even the "mutual aid" you mentioned must have meaning under certain conditions. Under the current deformed organization, it is impossible to talk about. But please don't misunderstand, we are not preventing people from doing "charity". We hope that everyone can do a broader and greater "charity" that can save everyone. Only this kind of "charitable fact" that can save everyone is "true" "charity". This is what we should tell you.

Sun Ruchang, please note: Your views are excellent, but they are not suitable for publication. Please provide your mailing address so that we can discuss them in a letter. We look forward to hearing from you!
