Education News Highlights

Shandong Province Joint Entrance Examination in Two Days

All Plans Have Been Defined

Chief Examiners Will Depart

(Jinan Correspondence) The Shandong Provincial Middle School Graduation Joint Entrance Examination will be held starting on the 16th of this month. Therefore, the Department of Education specially appointed the chief examiners for each district's middle school graduation joint entrance examination today (the 11th), and stipulated the joint entrance examination method, examination hall rules, and grade calculation method, notifying all responsible agencies to comply with them. As for the assistant examiners for each district's joint entrance examination, they will be appointed from competent talents within each district. It is also heard that the examination committee members of each district, as the examination is very near, will go to their respective districts tomorrow or the day after tomorrow to quickly prepare for the examination. The list of chief examiners for each district and various rules are recorded below.

List of Chief Examiners

Yantai District: Inspector Xu Yuanliang; Wendeng District: Inspector Peng Rulin; Huangxian District: Inspector Wu Mingyu; Weixian District: Inspector Ma Rumei; Linqing District: Inspector Sun Fangshi; Linyi District: Instructor Feng Guangrong.

Joint Examination Methods

Article 1: All students from provincial, county, and registered private middle schools within the province who have completed their studies and achieved passing grades should take the joint examination held by the Department of Education. Article 2: The matters and deadlines for middle schools participating in the graduation joint examination to report are as follows: (1) Textbooks or self-compiled lecture notes and teaching progress schedules for each subject should be reported within one month after the start of the second semester of the third academic year. (2) Student registration books and grade reports for each subject of the academic year for graduating students should be reported to the department two weeks before the joint examination. (3) Each graduating student's 2.5-inch portrait photo should be collected and sent to the department one month before the joint examination. (4) Each graduating student's conduct grades for each academic year should be reported to the department one week before the joint examination. Article 3: The Department of Education should divide the province into several districts according to the number of graduating classes in each middle school, and select a suitable place in each district as the joint examination location. Article 4: The date of the graduation joint examination should be determined by the Department of Education and held simultaneously in each district. Article 5: The chief and assistant examiners for each district should be appointed or commissioned by the Department of Education. Article 6: The invigilators for each district should be appointed or commissioned by the Department of Education from personnel in administrative or judicial agencies in each district. Article 7: The proctors should be appointed or commissioned by the Department of Education, except for teachers and staff from the schools participating in the examination. Article 8: The seating arrangement for each examinee should be mixed and distributed, with one person per table as the principle. The examination hall rules will be determined separately. Article 9: The exam questions for each subject should be prepared in duplicate by the proctors and sent to the Director of Education for determination, sealed and brought by each chief examiner, and opened on the spot in each district. Article 10: The exam papers for each subject should be prepared by the Department of Education and should not be sealed. Article 11: After collecting the exam papers for each subject, the chief examiner and invigilator should check the number, tear off the floating tags, seal them tightly, stamp them with their names, and send them to the Department of Education. Article 12: The grading of the exam papers for each subject is divided into three types: initial grading, review grading, and final grading. The initial and review grading are the responsibility of the proctors, and the final grading is personally performed by the Director of Education. Article 13: The calculation of grades for each subject will be determined separately. Article 14: After the joint examination grades are determined, the Department of Education should announce them separately in accordance with the provisions of Article 11 of the Ministry's Provisional Regulations on the Joint Examination of Graduates of Primary and Secondary Schools. Article 15: If a student's joint examination grade is failing in one or two subjects, they may retake the subjects once. The retake method is the same as the joint examination. Article 16: If there are any omissions in this method, the Department of Education should revise them at any time and report them for record. Article 17: This method will be implemented from the date of approval and promulgation.

Examination Hall Rules

(1) Examinees should go to the examination hall according to the number on the floating tag of the examination paper and take their seats according to the number. (2) Examinees should obey the orders of the examination committee. (3) Examinees should not bring books or papers into the examination hall. (4) Do not make noise or recite aloud. (5) Do not whisper to each other. (6) Do not peek at other people's exam papers. (7) Do not ask for explanations of the exam questions. (8) Scratch paper is provided at the end of the paper. Do not use separate paper. Scratch paper and exam paper should be submitted together. (9) Do not exceed the time limit for submitting the paper. (10) After submitting the paper, do not request to add or change words. (11) Do not re-enter the examination hall after leaving. (12) If an examinee has irregular behavior and is found by the examination committee, all grades will be invalidated.

Method for Calculating Joint Examination Grades

(1) Calculate the grades for each subject using the percentage method. Round off decimals below the whole number using the rounding rule. (2) A grade of 80 or above in each subject is considered A; 70 to 79 is considered B; 60 to 69 is considered C; 59 or below is considered D. (3) A, B, and C are passing grades; D is a failing grade. (4) The total average score of each subject is the joint examination grade. (5) The result of averaging the three-year average score and the joint examination grade is the graduation grade. (6) Conduct grades are calculated separately and are not averaged with the other subjects, etc.

Huang Linsheng Succeeds as Supervisor of Students Studying in Japan

Nanjing, 13th: The Ministry of Education has appointed Huang Linsheng to succeed as Supervisor of Students Studying in Japan.

Qingdao Schools Military Training Review

Qingdao, 13th: The Education Bureau has scheduled a military training review of all levels of schools for the afternoon of the 14th. A total of 16 schools, approximately 2,700 people, will participate.

Senior High School Curriculum Standards (8)

Biology

I. Objectives

(1) To enable students to understand the basic principles of life phenomena.

(2) To enable students to understand the morphology, structure, and life functions of animals and plants.

(3) To enable students to understand the essentials of genetics and the theory of evolution.

(4) To enable students to understand the general outline of the classification of the animal and plant kingdoms and Chinese specialties.

(5) To enable students to understand the relationship between animals and plants and their environment.

(6) To enable students to understand the position of human beings in the natural world.

II. Time Allocation

To be taught in the first academic year of senior high school, with three hours of lectures and two hours of experiments per week. In addition, several field collections can be held each semester.

III. Curriculum Outline

(1) Characteristics of living organisms.

(2) Similarities and differences between animals and plants.

(3) Significance of studying biology.

(4) Methods of studying biology.

(5) Branches of biology and their developmental history.

(6) Relationship between biology and other sciences.

(7) Cells and protoplasm (1) Microscopic observation of protoplasm; (2) Chemical composition of protoplasm; (3) Compounds that make up protoplasm; (4) Physical properties of protoplasm; (5) Structure of cells; (6) Cell division; 1. Direct division; 2. Indirect division.

(8) Tissues and organs (1) Differentiation and aggregation of cells; (2) Tissues that make up the plant body; (3) Tissues that make up the animal body; (4) Organs that make up plants; (5) Organs that make up animals; (6) Similarity and homology of organs.

(9) Nutrition (1) Metabolism of plants; 1. Chlorophyll and photosynthesis; 2. Formation of protoplasm; 3. Respiration and energy change; 4. Roots and rhizomes and metabolism; (2) Metabolism of animals; 1. Animal feeding habits; 2. Digestion of food; 3. Absorption of food; 4. Respiration; 5. Excretion; 6. Circulation; (3) Circulation of various substances in nature; 1. Carbon cycle; 2. Nutrient cycle; 3. Nitrogen cycle.

(10) Sensitivity (1) Sensitivity of plants; (2) Nervous system of animals; (3) Sensory organs of animals; (4) Internal secretion of animals.

(11) Reproduction (1) Significance of reproduction; (2) Methods of various types of reproduction; 1. Asexual reproduction: Binary fission, budding, spore formation, conjugation; 2. Sexual reproduction; 3. Parthenogenesis (i.e., virgin birth); 4. Paedogenesis (i.e., reproduction by larvae); (3) Alternation of generations; 1. Alternation of generations in mosses; 2. Alternation of generations in ferns; 3. Alternation of generations in seed plants; 4. Alternation of generations in the animal kingdom; 5. Metamorphosis.

(12) Development (1) Origin of gametes; (2) Maturation and meiosis of gametes; (3) Morphology of gametes; (4) Fertilization; (5) Development of plants; (6) Development of animals; (7) Haeckel's law of recapitulation and its limitations.

(13) Heredity (1) Pre-Mendelian concepts of heredity; (2) Mendel's law; (3) Material basis of heredity; (4) Sex-linked inheritance.

(14) Evolution (1) Theory of evolution; (2) Evidence of evolution; (3) Adaptation; 1. Functional adaptation; 2. Structural adaptation; 3. Mutual adaptation between organisms; (4) Evolution of mankind.

(15) Classification (Pay attention to Chinese products) (1) Methods of classification; (2) Outline of plant classification and its geographical distribution; Outline of animal classification and its geographical distribution.

(16) Relationship between animals and plants and human life.

IV. General Implementation Methods

(1) Work Items

(1) Lectures: Based on the above objectives, select a suitable senior high school biology textbook and lecture and discuss with students in the classroom.

(2) Practice: In the laboratory, 1. Use simple instruments and materials to test various physiological phenomena; 2. Use a microscope to observe various animal and plant sections and tissues, draw diagrams and indicate their parts; 3. Dissect various animals and plants, understand their structure, and compare their similarities and differences; 4. Collect animal and plant specimens in the suburbs, identify their types, and investigate their environment.

(2) Key Teaching Points

(1) Students must obtain basic and correct concepts about life phenomena.

(2) Students must be able to corroborate what they have seen in practice with the theories taught.

(3) Students must develop the ability to study independently and an interest in nature.

(4) Students must be trained in scientific methods (such as observation, experimentation, comparison, classification, etc.). Emphasis should not be placed on drawing diagrams.

Local News

The French Municipal Council's Indication on Subsidies for Private Schools

Individual Requests Should Be Given Special Consideration

The Private School Federation Still Needs to Continue its Efforts

Regarding the case of the Shanghai French Concession Private Primary and Secondary School Federation requesting subsidies from the French Municipal Council for private schools within the concession, the French Municipal Council issued a notice yesterday, clearly stating that the Private School Federation believes there has been no result and still needs to continue its efforts. The details are recorded as follows:

Municipal Council Notice: The French Municipal Council issues the following notice: This council recently received a letter from the French Concession Private Primary and Secondary School Federation requesting subsidies. This council has always attached importance to public education, and the issue of moral education is of particular concern to the French Concession authorities. Therefore, this council has not only allocated substantial funds to establish various Chinese children's schools, but also subsidized significant amounts to various Chinese educational institutions within the concession in the form of grants or tax exemptions. Furthermore, in 1931, a new Chinese children's school was established, with establishment costs reaching 300,000 yuan, and annual operating expenses reaching 22,222 taels of silver, all borne by this council's budget, which is clear evidence of this council's greatest efforts. This council will certainly give special and fair consideration to individual private schools that come to request subsidies. This notice is hereby issued.

The Private School Federation's Statement: According to Mr. Ma Jia, a standing committee member of the federation, speaking to a Shanghai News reporter yesterday, after the Municipal Government and the Municipal Bureau of Education agreed to be responsible for contacting the French Consul-General for negotiations regarding the federation's subsidy request, it immediately complied with the order to temporarily suspend its efforts and await the outcome. This notice from the French Municipal Council, although a public announcement, has not been formally received by the federation. The federation does not consider it a reply, and the expressions within the notice cannot be considered a result. Therefore, the private schools within the concession are awaiting the outcome and holding examinations, which has delayed this matter. It has now been decided to convene a general meeting in the shortest possible time to jointly discuss how to proceed, and it is planned to expand the movement.

Hu Bei Middle School Approved for Registration

Qiujiang Road Hu Bei Middle School was established in 1918. Later, due to a dispute over the demolition of houses in Yile Lane, it was forced to suspend operations. In the autumn of 1929, the board of directors was reorganized and continued to run a junior high school. Over the years, the student body has grown and the results have been remarkable. During the Shanghai War, the school site was appropriately located in the line of fire, resulting in significant losses. After the ceasefire and takeover, the school was relocated to 587 opposite the street, a four-story Western-style building, with spacious houses. Every effort was made to add various facilities to improve the school. A sports field was added, and a library was built to focus on management and actively restore the school. Recently, an application was submitted to the Municipal Bureau of Education for registration. After sending personnel to inspect, it was deemed qualified and approved at the bureau's meeting on the 10th of this month, and submitted to the Ministry of Education for record. It is reported that the school is scheduled to open on February 1st, and there has been a very enthusiastic response from all parties applying for enrollment.

The private Pei Ying Girls' Primary School in Tongchang Lane, Haining Road, Zhabei District, has been established for three years. Ms. Zhao Yanrong, the principal, has done considerable research on early childhood education. Now, in order to develop early childhood education, a kindergarten will be added starting next semester. The matter has been submitted to the Municipal Bureau of Education for approval and record.

Sports

London to Have Nighttime Electric Football

Approved by the English Football Association

(London Correspondence) Those who have long desired to hold nighttime electric football matches now seem to have achieved their final victory. The English Football Association Council has agreed to hold a football match under electric light at the White City Stadium. The official date has not yet been determined, but the important point is that the Council has changed its mind. In 1930, when there was a request to hold electric football, the Council firmly replied that such a competition was undesirable and prevented members from participating. Even with threats, this state remained until the Waldorf team and the London United teams renewed their request, which led to the current result. This White City Stadium can accommodate 50,000 spectators and is now the home field of the Queens Park Rangers team, a Division Three team in the London United League.

Today's Football Match Canceled Due to Snow and Ice

Tomorrow's Intercity Trial Match Undecided

Yesterday, the Western Union Football Association issued a notice stating that due to the heavy snowfall in recent days and the accumulation of snow on the field, reaching several inches in thickness, all football matches scheduled for today have been canceled. Whether tomorrow's (Sunday) intercity trial match to be held at the China Baseball Field can proceed as usual will depend on the weather conditions today. In addition, the China Football Association's matches scheduled for today have also been canceled.

Hong Kong Intercity Trial Match

The Lineup is Roughly Determined for the 26th

John's High School Wins Again in the Western YMCA B-League Final to Defend the Championship

52-25 | In Two A-League Games, John's Heavily Defeats Xia Guang, Jinan Heavily Defeats Jiang Wan

John's High School won the Western YMCA Basketball B-League Championship. Last night, in the second game of the final, John's defeated Wanxing 38-29, winning both games and thus winning the championship. There were also two A-League games last night: (1) John's heavily defeated Xia Guang 64-29; (2) Jinan heavily defeated Jiang Wan 45-15.

John's Wins Again Against Wanxing

Wanxing Takes the Initiative Wanxing had great momentum at the beginning of the game, opening the scoring with a 2-0 lead. John's responded immediately.

However, Wanxing's Li Silin's long shot and Wang Jilu's free throw gave Wanxing a commanding 5-2 lead. John's counterattacked and scored four consecutive points to tie the game at 6-5. But Wanxing took the lead again with a 7-6 score.

One Point Alternates Up and Down After John's took a 6-5 lead, Wanxing countered with a 7-6 lead. For the next five minutes, it was a difficult and inseparable era, with the score alternating up and down three or four times. John's Ma Fangcui scored in the middle, giving John's an 8-7 lead. Then came 8-9, 10-9, 10-11, 12-11, until 12-11, when John's took a one-point lead, and the situation suddenly opened up.

John's Continues to Sail Smoothly At 14-11, Wanxing took a break, but Ma Fangcui and Zhang Yuanji scored four more points in a row. With such momentum, Wanxing suddenly showed signs of shaking and the line became chaotic. John's was unstoppable, reaching 25-11. The result of the first half was 29-14. In the second half, Wanxing still did not show any improvement. At the end of the game, the score was 52-25. John's High School won again and won the championship.

Regulations for the Ministry of Education Summer Physical Education Training Class

The Ministry of Education announced the summer physical education training class on the 12th, which was reported yesterday. The 25 articles of the regulations are listed below:

Chapter 1 General Provisions Article 1: In order to train physical education personnel and promote national physical education, the Ministry of Education will hold a summer physical education training class (hereinafter referred to as "the class") from July 10 to August 20, 1933. Article 2: The class will be located at the Central University in the capital.

Chapter 2 Preparatory Committee Article 3: The preparatory work for the class will be handled by the preparatory committee. Article 4: The preparatory committee will consist of five to seven members, appointed by the Ministry of Education. Article 5: The preparatory committee will have one executive member to handle daily affairs. Article 6: The preparatory committee will have several secretaries and clerks, who will be hired separately or concurrently by faculty and staff members of the Central University, subject to the discretion of the Ministry of Education. Article 7: The detailed rules of the preparatory committee will be determined separately. Article 8: The preparatory committee will be dissolved upon the establishment of the summer physical education training class.

Chapter 3 Organization Article 9: The class will have one director to preside over all matters, appointed by the Ministry of Education. Article 10: The class will have two groups, general affairs and academic affairs, each with one director and several members, appointed by the class. Article 11: The responsibilities of each group are as follows: (1) The general affairs group will be responsible for document accounting, administrative affairs and matters not belonging to other groups. (2) The academic affairs group will be responsible for curriculum preparation, registration, training, and other matters related to academic affairs. Article 12: The class may set up different levels according to the students' level and the nature of the specialized subjects. The method will be determined by the preparatory committee and reported to the Ministry of Education for record. Article 13: The teachers of the class will be appointed by the director. Article 14: The teachers of the class will be honorary positions, but travel expenses and allowances may be provided at the discretion of the class. Article 15: The class may employ several staff members as needed. Article 16: The detailed rules of the class will be determined separately.

Chapter 4 Admission Qualifications Article 17: The number of students in the class is temporarily set at 300. Article 18: The students of the class will be recommended by the education departments and bureaus of each province and city, including current physical education teachers in primary and secondary schools, physical education staff, instructors from martial arts schools, or those who have considerable research and interest in physical education. The preparatory committee will review and admit the students.

Chapter 5 Personnel and Tuition Article 19: When recommending students, the education departments and bureaus of each province and city must submit a form detailing each student's academic qualifications and experience to the preparatory committee for review before May 1, 1933. After receiving the notice of qualification, they will instruct the students to attend school. Article 20: Each student will pay a tuition fee of 20 yuan. Article 21: Students are responsible for their own meals and accommodation. The methods for those who live and eat at the school will be determined separately. Article 22: Students will be responsible for compensating for any damage to school equipment and sports equipment. Chapter 6 Curriculum and Graduation Article 23: The curriculum will be based on the provisions of the "National Physical Education Implementation Plan Teacher Training" item, and will be adjusted according to the purpose of training and the allocation of time. The preparatory committee will decide and report to the Ministry of Education for record. Article 24: Students who complete the training period and pass the examination will be issued a certificate by the class and reported to the Ministry of Education for record. Chapter 7 Supplementary Provisions Article 25: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they will be amended by the Ministry of Education.

The Inauguration of the Shanghai Chinese Sports Club

The building is scheduled to open on May 1st, and everything is officially established and is actively progressing

The development of sports in Shanghai is the best in the country, but the organization of sports clubs has never been heard of. On the Western side, there are the Race Club, the Country Club, etc. Although their purpose is not purely to promote sports, they also promote various sports with great effort. Recently, many enthusiastic sports enthusiasts in China have realized the lack of such an organization, and thus initiated the establishment of a sports club. It was officially announced at 5:30 PM this Thursday at the Dahua Apartment on Jing'an Temple Road. However, the Chinese name has not yet been finalized, while the Western name is National Recreation Club. The initial purpose is to promote tennis, with the establishment of 15 tennis courts. In the future, it is planned to gradually expand. The economic aspect has been settled, and a building will be built on Daxilu Road. It is scheduled to officially open on May 1st of this summer. All affairs are being actively prepared by the organizing committee. This type of organization, which emphasizes both sports and entertainment, is still a first in Shanghai and deserves attention. The details are explored as follows:

Founders

Cheng Yize, Zhang Yuelian, Wei Boxiang, Zheng Zirong, Sun Linfang, Dong Dayou,

Li Baojun, Xi Jingyong, Xu Zhixiang, Chen Sanjiu, Wang Zhongwei, Huang Xuanping, Jiang Daozhang, Gu Qinghuang, Gu Qingyi, Chen Shuxun, Li Lei, Lu Pinqin, Li Zuhe, Tong Yuwen, Shen Liren, Cai Shi'an, Yuan Qiuchu, Zhang Zengpei, Zheng Huan, He Shuiyuan, Liang Guanliu

Organizing Committee

The organizing committee has been established, with Zhang Yuelian elected as the chairman of the organizing committee, and Jiang Daozhang as the secretary. The organizing committee members are Wei Boxiang, Sun Linfang, Dong Dayou, Li Baojun, Chen Sancai, Gu Qinghuang, and He Yongyuan. All affairs are actively underway. In the future, an executive committee will also be organized, and an executive secretary will be elected to preside over all affairs.

Membership Types

Membership is not limited to those interested in sports, including general, female, and student memberships. The entrance fee for general members is 30 yuan, and the annual fee is 40 yuan. The entrance fee for female members is 10 yuan, and the annual fee is 12 yuan. Student memberships are temporary, because schools must take vacations and cannot stay in Shanghai for a long time. Therefore, there is no entrance fee, only a monthly fee of 3 yuan. The budget assumes 400 general members, and 60 female and student members each. Together with other income from food and beverages, etc., this is enough to cover the annual expenses (the annual budget is less than 20,000 yuan). It is reported that there are already 300 general members.

Construction Costs

The location has been decided as on Great West Road, to construct a two-story Western-style building of 100 feet long and 50 feet wide. Dong Dayou has already planned the construction, with an estimated cost of approximately 20,000 yuan. Funding is also secured, planning to issue 20,000 yuan in public bonds to be subscribed by various promoters. Some are subscribing for 1,000 yuan, while others are subscribing for 500 yuan. The interior will include a banquet hall, dressing rooms, cloakrooms, shower rooms, etc. The lawn and hard tennis courts will have at least fifteen courts. The project is scheduled to be completed by the end of April this year and officially open on May 1st, it is said.

Spring and Autumn

Ceylonese Fire-Walking Ceremony

— Zhan Lu

— One of the World's Exotic Customs and Ballads —

"Exploring Boiling Water and Walking on Fire" has been said since ancient times, this is a metaphor, not a fact; unexpectedly in Ceylon across the two oceans, the people there have the art of fire-walking. Every year when the Aissala Festival arrives, [Note 1] which is July 17th, a grand ceremony is held for fire-walking, and the spectators are densely packed. A wide square is specially prepared in front of the temple, dry firewood is stacked into a bridge-like structure, and asphalt and tung oil are poured over and over again, intending to increase the burning power. There is a priest in charge of this, who determines when to start and when to finish burning. The burning starts from noon and ends in the early evening, the timing is crucial and must not be missed! The chief priest suddenly gives the order to ignite, and in an instant, it blazes fiercely; the worshippers burn the fire, worship, and sing, their attire is strange and varied. They bare their arms and perform a demonic dance together, chanting Sanskrit verses of "Prajnaparamita"; they walk barefoot, their movements erratic, sometimes slow, sometimes fast. Once the dancing is over, the fire-walking begins, initiated voluntarily, not by coercion; perhaps because they have offended the sacred deity, or because of personal misdeeds; once they desire to redeem their past sins, only fire-walking can wash them away. Before the chief priest gives the order to fire-walk, they stand before him with bowed hands; he bestows upon them the rituals and incantations, and then orders them to bathe to show purity. Once the chief priest gives the order to fire-walk, they walk barefoot, unafraid of the scorching heat; they lift their robes and step onto the burning embers, walking calmly, observing the precepts. At this time, the setting sun is just about to disappear behind the mountains, with red clouds scattered across the sky; but how can the red clouds compare to the red of the burning embers? People retreat from several feet away; only those fire-walkers remain. What is the meaning of their heroic and outstanding demeanor? To walk on fire without being burned is considered the only glory; otherwise, if the burning embers injure their skin, it indicates that the deity's anger has not yet been appeased; walking on and on until they reach the end of the ritual platform, [Note 2] the fire-walking ceremony is then declared complete; they compete to prostrate themselves before the deity, chanting Sanskrit hymns that soar through the clouds, their spirit resolute to this extent! When I hear of this, I sigh deeply! Now that the national crisis is upon us, how dare we indulge in comfort? If everyone embraces the spirit of fire-walking, perhaps this great calamity can be averted; otherwise, if we continue to dance and sing in revelry, we will sit and watch our homeland change colors, and once the conflagration ignites, what will become of us? Our Buddha only says: "It cannot be spoken of."

Note 1: Aissala means reverence for the gods, the Aissala Festival is the Festival of Reverence.

Note 2: Sgangda is the deity worshiped in Ceylon.

Snow

— Huo Xueming

— Poet and Dog —

After a day of warm rain, the weather cleared at dusk, followed by cold wind with sharp edges. The sky was full of yellow clouds, looking like it was about to snow. Finally, the earth turned completely white.

It is said that dogs love snow because they can see their own plum blossom-shaped footprints. However, I believe that poets love snow even more than dogs; because cooking wine in the icy weather and writing poetry amidst a white battlefield are elegant activities recognized and respected by noble scholars throughout history.

Bai Juyi's "Evening comes, the sky threatens snow, would you drink a cup with me?" captures the mood of awaited snow. Wang Wei's "Wind startles bamboo outside the window, opening the door, snow fills the mountain; scattering into the deep silent alley, accumulating white in the wide courtyard" captures the mood of admiring the snow when it falls. As for Cen Shen's Tian Shan Snow Song and White Snow Song, such magnificent and grand poetic realms are no less than Li Bai's "Heavenly soldiers shining in the snow descend Yuguan" and "Yan Mountain snowflakes are as big as mats," both capturing the mood of fighting amidst the snow in the northern regions. Now, amidst the red shadows of the island barbarians concentrating and shedding blood in Yuguan, there drifts swirling frozen snow, and our anti-Japanese heroes are in a season where "the general lies in fox fur, but cannot keep warm"! But what about our poets?

The relationship between snow and poets is as sweet as honey, so closely linked. Fan Chengda said, "It's not that charcoal must be sent in the snow, but to add scenery for poetry," which says it all.

Perhaps it is because the purity of snowflakes symbolizes the noble integrity of scholars, or perhaps it is because snow only falls in the harsh winter, believing that it possesses an aura of unyielding pride, that it is especially loved, which is also unknown. Chinese poets have always praised the importance of having an unyielding spirit in life.

As for why dogs are more excited in snowy weather, I believe that they run wildly on the snow, and besides the explanation of warming up, I cannot know any further. What is the meaning of young men and women skating on the solid ice of Beihai? I also cannot know.

Here, let me copy a poem about dogs and snow by Mr. Zhang Dayou of the Song Dynasty to end this short essay. The poem says:

"The universe is one chaotic whole, the ancient well a dark cave, yellow dog has white on it, white dog is swollen." Mr. Liu Dabai said about this poem: "Such descriptive means are truly admirable and astonishing; I am afraid that even the snow-praising poems of the great masters cannot achieve this!"

Symbolism of Flowers

— Ren Ying

— Fresh Blood and Freedom —

Two pots of unnamed flowers have been added to the flower stand, adorning the long corridor. Yesterday, as I dragged my tired body past, I noticed them in front of the flower stand. Slender petals, as crimson as blood, surrounded by delicate green leaves; I stood in silence before the flower stand.

Don't the crimson petals symbolize the unrestrained flow of fresh blood? Don't the tender green leaves symbolize liberation and freedom? The region south of the Yangtze River is shrouded in bright spring light, while the distant northern land, on the paths of ice and snow, sees the undulating movement of the nation's brave warriors. And in that vast, cold sky, amidst the deep snow, enemy iron birds are soaring. Splashing mud, blurred bloodstains, they are sacrificing their individual selves for the struggle of the entire nation! In the Heilong River, the blood tide of martyrs surges, and on Changbai Mountain, the corpses of heroes pile up. Enduring hunger and cold, forsaking family and fortune, isn't what they are hoping for the same as the green leaves of freedom?

To strive for the nation's freedom, the blood flowers of brave warriors must bloom. Flow, flow, let the unrestrained blood of the Chinese nation flow to the last drop. Hope, hope, hope for the green leaves bathing in the spring light.

When the bloodstains of the brave warriors receive their due price. In that not-so-distant tomorrow, next to the blood-like petals, will be the contrasting green of freedom. Let us create, at the forefront of that era; leave behind the fragrance of history.

Seeking Justice

— Zi Tai

— Justice Found for the God of War —

Justice had disappeared from the celestial realm, causing great panic among the gods; because their realm relied entirely on justice for its maintenance, and without justice, their realm would collapse.

Therefore, the gods of the celestial realm convened an emergency meeting to discuss the matter of finding justice. In the meeting hall, the God of Peace first stood up and spoke, saying that he was willing to do his best to find justice to safeguard the celestial realm. Later, the God of War followed, also saying, like the God of Peace, that he would retrieve justice. The gods, terrified by the disappearance of justice, immediately agreed to them upon hearing that these two great gods were willing to exert their efforts, and set them a deadline of three days to respond.

Three days later, the God of Peace was the first to respond. He said that he could not find justice. Because every place he went, he asked if they were hiding justice, or if justice had taken refuge there, and they all rejected him fiercely. Now, there was no way, and he had to return empty-handed. He begged for the forgiveness of the gods.

What about the God of War? He came to answer in no time. He said that he had already found justice. Because every place he went, he ultimately used all his military force to search and find it, no matter how they refused; finally, in one place, he found the disappeared justice. As he spoke, he showed the gods the justice he had found.

The celestial realm was therefore restored to peace. The gods were all relieved of their fear.

From this, they realized that only war can retrieve justice; and only war can proclaim justice to people.

Fisherman

— Yellow Poplar Woodcut

Novel

Guilty Conscience

— Liao Hongshou Juan

So he thought in confusion again: What if he couldn't get through this long snowy journey tonight? What then? When he arrived at his destination, what if he couldn't wake the deep sleep of the people in the house, what then? Even if he woke them up, what if they were unwilling to brave the cold to open the door, what then? If that were really the case, would he still have the courage to brave the wind and snow of more than ten miles to rush home again? Even if it were possible to rush home, would he still have the courage to face his stepmother's icy and cold face? If he didn't have this courage and went to other relatives and friends, would they not find him annoying in such cold weather and such a late night? Even if people weren't annoyed, would he be able to get such sincere and enthusiastic treatment? ... He thought blankly and couldn't help but mutter: 'Oh, oh, I'm afraid not! Oh, oh, it certainly won't!'

As soon as his mind recovered a little, his thoughts were more numerous than weeds under the spring breeze. He thought about what he should think about and what he shouldn't. The torrent of thoughts was surging, unable to be pushed away or discarded. As a result, he only felt that countless cells and blood in his whole body were completely filled with indescribable emotions of gratitude. He desperately wanted to find a set of tearful words of gratitude to express a little gratitude to his good friend, but after searching his brain, he couldn't even string together half a suitable sentence. In the end, he seemed unable to utter even the most common word 'thank you'. He just raised his bright but dull eyes and looked at them warmly. His eyes were full of tears, about to drip but not yet dripping.

Dongfang Sheng was his classmate before, and now he is only in his twenties. He is a broad-minded youth who inclines towards nature. His state is very heroic, and in his heroism, he carries a look of kindness and amiability. He was originally a model Christian, with the same universal loving heart as God. On the other hand, the gentleness of his actions is like that of a Buddhist believer. All these things are enough to match his kind appearance and are not like some people in the world who are outwardly good but inwardly filthy.

Dongfang Sheng's wife, Xiao Man, is only three or five years younger than Dongfang Sheng, but her appearance, expression, behavior, and speech are still completely like those of a young girl with her hair in pigtails. She carries a bit of innocence everywhere, and it is revealed naturally from time to time. She sits next to her husband, just like a lively and endearing little bird. Because she just got out of bed, her beautiful hair is fluffy, her sleepiness hasn't dissipated, and both cheeks are slightly flushed like the buds of a Chinese flowering crabapple from the warmth of the stove. Her expression contains kindness in liveliness, which is the same point between her and her husband. Especially her slightly sleepy but clear eyes, like autumn water, whenever they look at her face, her eyes seem to emit a warm and kind voice, as if saying: 'Alas! Poor person, poor child, why have you gotten into such a mess?' (5)

World Oddities

Predictions for the Future of 1933

— Special

The well-known French seer Madame Fraya predicted that President Hoover would fail in the election, that White Star An would end, that the postal ship George Maliba would burn, and that Doumer would be killed, all of which came true last year. Now that the old year has passed and the new year is approaching, she calculates that the future of the coming year is bleak. She said:

In 1933, we will still not be able to escape economic hardship. There will be many financial collapses in Europe and America. In the first few months of this year, relations between the United States and France will be tense, but they may gradually improve later. The year's luck for England is quite bad, and the harm to the pound will almost last throughout the year. Major changes will occur in India and other dependent territories. A politician in France will be in danger of assassination. A new figure will rise to power in France, and after he emerges, business will begin to turn around. His achievements are many, but they are mostly achieved through diplomatic means. Germany is actively preparing for war, and France is in danger of being attacked, but the attack will not be realized. The East is in a troubled autumn.

In the first few months of 1933, there will be great storms and disasters in the sky and at sea. Science will make great progress, and there will be extraordinary discoveries in medicine. A great leader in Germany will disappear from the political scene. Two politicians and two writers in France will depart from this world.

Spanish policy will take two decisive turns to the left. Relations between France and Italy will be more friendly than at the beginning of the year. Russian Bolshevism will suffer a major blow, and its political system will be shaken. After a battle, its policy will turn to a more peaceful Bolshevism.

Italy's fortune is very good, and its development will be even more brilliant. Latin America will remain turbulent, Argentina's finances can be expected to be stable, but a political revolution will occur within the country. Women in various countries will become more prominent. Much capital will change hands, and people in the middle class will suffer everywhere, leading to various incidents, but there will be no revolutions in France and North America.

After Roosevelt defeated Hoover in the American presidential election, Madame Fraya received hundreds of letters from the United States congratulating her on the complete accuracy of her predictions for 1932.

··················

Also, the Syrian Muhammad Shek, who lives in Cairo, the capital of Egypt, is famous for his stargazing. He predicts that in 1933, there will be war between France and Italy, with England assisting France, but it will encounter misfortune. The Balkans will be greatly affected as a result. There will be more chaos in Mexico, which will eventually be annexed by the United States. China and Japan will still not officially go to war, but they will still fight sporadic battles, resulting in an agreement of some kind. Other places, such as Iraq, Yemen, and Palestine, will all have some wars. In short, the future situation is very difficult, and there will be many disasters, it is said.

According to these two seers, their words about Franco-Italian relations are completely opposite. It is really not known which one is accurate, so we will wait until the end of the year to determine it.

Testing Human Nature

— Yi An

Lyon Berra of Marseille, France, wanting to test how his friends felt about him, suddenly issued a death notice and pretended to be dead and lay stiff in a coffin. When a group of friends gathered for the funeral, thinking that a final judgment had been made, they commented on the deceased's life. After Lyon Berra had finished listening to their words, he slowly got up from the coffin and thanked his friends. One person was so frightened that he died on the spot. The deceased's wife then sued Lyon Berra in court.

The Price of a Dead Tiger

— Yi An

The Yaoao region of India is plagued by tigers. In 1931, 85 people died from tigers. The more fortunate residents of this area are those of the class that has spears or firearms, for if they have these weapons, they can hunt and kill the tigers. Every time they catch a tiger, they first get a reward from the government, ranging from ten to twenty-five pounds. The tiger meat is then sold to the Chinese, for the Chinese in the south mostly love to eat tiger meat, believing that it can increase energy and strengthen muscles and bones. The fat is sold to the Indians for medicinal use to treat rheumatism. The bones and tiger claws can be made into ornaments, which fetch a high price. The tiger liver is sold to warriors, who say that eating it can increase courage. If it is a tigress, then her milk is said to be able to treat eye diseases. As for the tiger skin, it is sold to Europeans returning home. Statistics show that the value of a tiger can keep a hunter warm and fed for life.

The Terrifying Shrinking Wind of Copper Coins

Shrinking by 7,000 pieces, totaling 10,000 pieces this week

Cash Concentration, Flat Interest Rates, No Hope for Turnaround

The end of the lunar year is approaching, and the period for closure is imminent. The phenomenon of silver dollars increasing in value is becoming more apparent, and the concentration of cash is even greater than usual. Therefore, there is no possibility of a turnaround in the market price for interest rates. The economic situation in various commercial sectors is becoming even more strained. It is observed that in the past month or two, the prices of various goods have been unusually low, which is actually due to the rush to sell goods for cash, rather than due to cheaper sources. The tension in the external silver market can be seen from this.

Silver Dollar Interest Rates Fall, Silver Discounts Remain the Same

The early market interest rate for silver dollars remains the same as before, at 7 qian 1 fen 3 li 7 hao 5 si. Gradually Improving Standard Yarn and Cotton

Intensifying the Boycott Work

The Future of Chinese Cotton Consumption Is Promising

Rain and Snow Intertwined, Sources Scarce

Cotton Market Buyers' Intentions Are Strong

The yarn market is trending up, but actual demand remains sluggish. Various merchant groups have weaker purchasing power due to economic reasons. Some foreign cotton has fallen by five or six yuan.

Foreign Cotton Falls More Than It Rises

Yesterday, the American cotton market was strong, but it softened at the close due to long position liquidation and Wall Street's weakness. Futures fell by one to three points, and spot prices were unchanged. British cotton futures fell by one or two points, and spot prices fell by five points. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell by five points. The Indian cotton market was firm and stable, with short covering in Pingguoer and Aomula. Pingguoer fell by 1.75 rupees, Aomula rose by 0.25 rupees, and Bailuoxi fell by 1.375 rupees. The original telegram, Green Left (12th telegram).

Grains

Little Rice Arrives Downriver Amidst Heavy Snow

| | Prices Increase Again by 1, 2, 3, or 4 Jiao Per Hu | |

(South Shanghai) Due to the continuous wind and snow yesterday, the source of supply was even more scarce, with only numbers 5 and 6 arriving. The remaining goods in Pudong saw an opportunity to tighten up, so the selling prices were chaotic, with increases of 3 to 4 jiao. These were all stores in urban and rural areas. However, the trading volume yesterday could not be considered formal. It is said that many rice boats were blocked by the wind in the Minhang area. If the wind and snow stop, they can all arrive in Shanghai one after another. It is thought that prices may be flattened somewhat at that time. Juyi did not open due to the decline in Tianjin prices and the lack of Bo rice. Only a few hundred shi of factory Bo rice were traded at the original prices. Xiangyang tips and Xiangyuan were both popular goods, but there was no large demand.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, ships numbered 32 and 33 arrived. White rice sales continued, and the market was even tighter. There were slightly more sources of Bo rice, and sales were still good, with prices standing firm. Early rice arrivals were scarce and sales were active. Du tips were scarce, while medium and lower grades were slightly available, and prices were tight. Yangbu tips were scarce, and sales were not bad, with prices increasing. Ke tips were also tight, and Baiyuan arrivals were not numerous, with retail sales being brisk and prices increasing again by 2 to 3 jiao.

Ke Yuan Is Out of Stock, Price Is High by Half a Yuan

Yesterday, Ke Yuan and Ke Xian arrivals were scarce. The market was originally looking good, and with few rice arrivals downriver, both northern and southern merchants had strong appetites. Yesterday, due to snow obstruction, the source of supply was even scarcer, and rice prices downriver rose and goods were scarce. Therefore, local hoarders focused on Ke Yuan. However, because the amount of Ke Yuan arriving recently was small, there was a need to build up stocks. Once local hoarders and both local and guest merchants competed to purchase, prices suddenly rose by half a yuan. Then, hoarders and local retailers purchased 669 bags of Hunan Zhong Yuan at prices as high as 10 yuan and 3 to 4 jiao. 586 bags of Wuhu machine-milled Yuan sold at prices as high as 10 yuan and 3 jiao to 4 jiao and a half, with medium grades at 9 yuan and 8 jiao 9 fen to 7 jiao and a half. Both northern and southern merchant demand was active. After the rice prices rose, attention turned to Ke Xian. It is estimated that northern merchants purchased 500 bags of Hunan machine-milled oil at prices ranging from 9 yuan and 5 fen to 9 yuan. Quanzhou merchants in the south purchased 550 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice at prices up to 9 yuan and 3 fen, both of which were up by 25 fen compared to the previous day. Sales were active and arrivals were scarce, and the outlook for the market remained good.

Vermicelli Market Guest Merchants Emerge

| | Reportedly Reaching 800,000 to 900,000 Bags | |

Yesterday in the vermicelli market, after the opening in the morning and afternoon, the market for each month showed a consistent downward trend. Foreign wheat quotations continued to decrease by about 2 to 3 jiao. Because the market sentiment was not good when the opening price was set in the morning, it was down by more than 1 fen compared to the previous day's closing price. Although the purchasing desire of actual sales merchants was tight, they were purchasing spot goods on one hand and closing out futures positions on the other. Within three or four days, guest merchants returned 800,000 to 900,000 bags of futures, which was huge. New account bulls were very limited, and even those who appeared to be bulls could not arouse market sentiment. In the afternoon, the market sentiment continued to weaken, because Australian wheat came into activity again. It was initially set to open at 3 taels and 7 qian, but later a new foreign firm managed to secure business, cheaply at 2 taels, 6 qian, 6 hao, and 8 and a half si. Factories and trading houses agreed to deliver three ships, mostly loaded with March goods. The continued weakness in market sentiment was due to this. As a result of the closing, the current month fell by 1 fen 7 li and a half compared to the previous day, February fell by 2 fen, March fell by 2 fen and 2 li and a half, April fell by 1 fen and 2 li and a half, May fell by 7 li and a half, and June fell by a few fen.

Yellow Soybeans Are Only Purchased by Domestic Factories

Although the yellow soybean market is fair, it is actually due to the approaching of the old year, so the situation is between two possibilities: going in or going out. Therefore, the current goods are slightly in consolidation. Yesterday, Kangjiageng entered three cars of Huaihai soybeans, one car of Zhengyangguan soybeans, 700 bags of Tushan soybeans, and one car of Wuhe soybeans. This was internal factory demand. Two packages of Pudong Du soybeans were traded by Guangdong merchants. Red sorghum sold two cars. The market belonged to a stable trend. Local merchants bought 56 bags of raw kernels, and the market showed great improvement. The oil situation was stable.

According to Reuters, London, 12th, Chinese horse beans rose sharply to 64.50 (per 120 pounds). Peanuts with shells rose slightly to 12.9, and shelled ones fell slightly to 14.50.

Chicago Wheat Falls Back

Xinhua Trading Company Report (12th), Chicago wheat fell by 0.625 to 1 point because the market rumored that the Far East entered 37 million bushels of Australian wheat. Also, the transaction number on the 11th was 40 million bushels. The market price on the 12th is listed below.

Silk and Tea

Compilation of Chinese and Foreign Silk Reports

(European and American Silk Telegrams Still Rarely Being Forwarded to Shanghai) Since the opening of various silk weaving factories in Europe and the United States in the New Year, Shanghai's yellow and white silk has been deemed too expensive, as the silk in hand is sufficient to meet demand. Yesterday morning, they were still rarely being forwarded to Shanghai, and the attitude of Chinese silk merchants remained idle. Existing silk transactions were still scarce.

(Antung Actively Stores Silk Before Forwarding to Shanghai) With the situation in Northeast China becoming increasingly tense, the silk stored in ports such as Antung and Yantai is now actively being forwarded to Shanghai. Yesterday, regular ships such as Dingsheng and others brought 184 pieces of raw silk to Shanghai.

(Sales of Artificial Silk Generally Remain Flat) Yesterday, the artificial silk market in Shanghai was flat because the Tianjin merchants stopped operations, and the Zhejiang and Shandong merchants were also idle because the closing period was approaching. Only local silk weaving factories purchased 32 boxes of Xingzhong Star brand artificial silk at a stable price.

(New York Raw Silk Sales Decline) Raw silk sales were sluggish last month (i.e., December). The American silk merchants in Shanghai received a telegram from the American Silk Association that the total amount of raw silk sold by silk weaving factories in the New York gold market in December was approximately 4548 packages. Among them, Japanese silk accounted for slightly less than 37,000 packages, Chinese silk accounted for only 2,952 packages, and the remainder was Italian and French raw silk.

Zhenmei Pearl Tea's Active Sales in France

Yesterday at the Shanghai tea market, Jardine Matheson, a British trading house, once again purchased Zhenmei pearl tea from both Luzhuang and Tuzhuang routes in large quantities. The spring sales in the Moroccan market were already active, and the tea prices in Shanghai were already extremely low. Therefore, transactions were quite strong, with total sales reaching 1,200 boxes. Most of them were Zhenmei from Wuyuan. As for the highest-quality goods in the northern route, because prices in Africa were tightening, Chinese merchants had a firm attitude, but there were still no large transactions.

North and South Goods

Daylily Market is Tightening Daily

Recently, because the market for daylilies is consistently tight, the trend is tightening daily. The current market price for goods from upper and middle merchants requires at least 14 taels before they are willing to sell. Therefore, merchants have been buying in recent days. Although there is some demand from sellers, they all want to buy cheaply. In order to reduce losses, only scattered transactions have been made. According to observations from people in the industry, there is hope that the price may reach 16 taels in the coming spring.

Metals

New Iron Wire Awaits Movement in Stillness

The trade in new iron wire has been sluggish for a long time. As a result, fellow traders all feel unmotivated to conduct business. The morning price is low, with No. 16 to No. 20 estimated at only 12 taels and 7 mace and 5 candareens per picul. Nos. 21, 23, and 15 are estimated at 13 taels and 2 mace. Aside from sporadic purchases for small-scale drawing, the market is essentially devoid of transactions. In recent days, there has been a sense of stillness awaiting movement. Dealers from Wenzhou, Sichuan, and Hankou have all made inquiries, and traders from Gu's group are also in negotiations. As a result, confidence has strengthened, and the market is on the rise, with prices expected to increase. It is reported that yesterday, 140 to 150 piculs were offered, with Nos. 16 to 20 priced at 13 taels and 5 mace per picul, and Nos. 21 to 25 priced at 14 taels per picul.

According to a Reuters dispatch from London on the 12th, tin has shown signs of weakness, lead has slightly risen, and tinplate remains unchanged. Also, according to a New York dispatch on the same day, tin and antimony have slightly risen, with tin at $22.875 per pound and antimony at $5.75.

Oil Market

Asphalt Inventory is Not Thick

丨Tung Oil Foreign Telegram Trends Downward丨

Since the continuous decline of asphalt in Hankou, the North and South have moved in opposite directions after the General Manager of the Zhejiang Railway. This kind of market situation is inherently accidental. The current new output is temporarily showing a sluggish trend, but it will not last long. Now, new goods from various brands in Hankou have arrived, and it is said that the new goods are superior to last year's old goods and the prices are lower, so sales are also moving. Heavy Jing is still at 12 taels and 7 or 8 mace, and Ordinary Jing is at 12 taels and 3 or 4 mace. High-quality Tianjin asphalt is at 12 taels, and slightly lower quality is at 11 taels and 8 or 9 mace. The price of Macheng oil once fell to 21 taels and 4 or 5 mace, but then rose by 1 mace and 4 candareens due to insufficient supply. The current market price is 11 taels and 7 or 8 mace, mainly because the Zhejiang Railway's prices are high, so they are all purchased from the Hankou market. However, sales in various places are lower than in previous years, which is due to the bankruptcy of the rural economy and the decline of all industries, not just one industry. Local merchants are buying and selling as they go. Although there are continuous arrivals of goods for both local and out-of-town merchants, they are enough to sell as they arrive, and there is rarely any accumulation. Fortunately, factories are not immediately purchasing goods, and are dedicated to supplying the candle-making market, so they are not in a state of destitution.

According to a Reuters dispatch from London on the 12th, tung oil fell by one penny to 38.6. Also, according to a New York dispatch on the same day, tung oil remains at 4.375.

Piece Goods

Light Woolen Fabric Market Remains Strong

Broadcloth, Watterine, Tweed

Although the sales season for imported woolen fabrics such as broadcloth, Watterine, and tweed has passed, those holding the goods are unwilling to sell them off, and the trend remains strong, mainly because the spring sales season will soon begin, and they are waiting for the prices to rise before selling them. Currently, Ningfeng checkered Watterine is selling for 2 taels, 9 mace, and 5 candareens net, Dafugui Suo Watterine is 3 taels and 2 mace, Pengshou Broadcloth is 2 taels and 4 mace, and Rongtai 15330 Laotou brand Constitutional Pattern Straight Tribute Cloth is 7 taels and 2 mace and 5 candareens, and Anli Jubao Basin is 5 taels and 8 mace.

Free Talk

Ten Years Later (2)

— Mo Ji

"But I failed, completely failed! Now I have to make a new decision, girl!"

"I know all about your struggles, I know all about them, ever since you left me." She remembered my past.

"Isn't that right," I said, "I left my apprenticeship to work in a factory, and when the factory closed down, I went to school. With my bare hands, I fought from east to west, and at that time I admired you so much! But my parents said that even if you struggled to go to school, you wouldn't be able to become an official after graduation! So you weren't qualified to have me. This place is filled with old gentry and rich men, so my parents sold me to them."

I paused at her words, with no room to refute them! She continued:

"I remember the past completely, I haven't forgotten a single thing: when you and I were close, you were already a complete slave. At first, you didn't resist at all, you lived your apprenticeship life meekly and obediently. But at that time I sympathized with you, I admired your ability to endure hardship, so when you brewed tea, I lit the fire for you, and when you cooked, I helped you. When I came to your store to play, you often came to my house too, and I helped you solve all your difficult problems; when you suffered insults and scolding from your boss, I tried to comfort you; when you injured your foot, I got you good food from my kitchen window. I nursed you, so that you could recover quickly. I treated you with such sincerity, completely from the bottom of my heart, and I wished to be close to you. So I didn't care when others said bad things about us. You ask me if I still have the you that I used to call 'brother' in my heart, please don't ask me that, because it makes me sad!

"Do you remember? I gave you my whole body: I hid it from my mother and let you kiss me, hug me, and——! You are a good person, I don't resent you at all, I wish you could jump from being a slave to being free, but now, you are still..."

"Just wishing that I alone could be free is not enough!..."

I also shed tears, hearing her words coming from her truly tender heart.

"You don't have to shed tears, dear! I haven't finished speaking yet:

"My parents said that their predictions were not wrong: you would not become an official. And indeed, now you don't even have a small job. I know you are starving, from slave to slave, that's what you are. Recently, I learned from books that you have many heavy stones on your shoulders! And on those stones stand many so-called 'rich people'. But I never imagined that Ying'er, who once sympathized with and helped you in your slave life, is now also standing on your shoulders. Please understand that I am pained by this! In these ten years of separation, I have often thought of you, but I could never see you again, so now, your image has finally become blurred; seeing you today, who would have known that you would be the you who has been destroyed, worn down, and tormented by the world and society for the past ten years!"

I stood by her bed, and hot tears dripped onto her dress. I was grateful that she could pity the weak person she had once sympathized with. I could only explain to her: (To be continued)

An Appeal for Peace

— Yang Xingzhi

Yesterday, this newspaper published an article by Mr. Wang Jingwei recently published in Geneva, urgently appealing for world peace. Mr. Wang's spirit of "loving peace" and "maintaining peace" is truly worthy of our sincere admiration.

However, what is the interpretation of the so-called "peace" at present? Mr. Wang seems to be a bit "feigning ignorance." In our view, in a world ruled by capitalist imperialism, the correct interpretation of peace is only the balance of power among the imperialist powers, only the intensified preparation for "plunder" and "armed conflict," and the disarmament conference meetings of generals and the League of Nations meetings of lords on peace are nothing more than a smoke screen to deceive the eyes and ears of the world's working masses. Therefore, the more vigorously the disarmament conference is held, the more frantically the military preparations of various countries expand, and the more anxiously the League of Nations conference ponders, the more the rumors of secret Anglo-Japanese and Franco-Japanese agreements spread throughout the world. Napoleon put it well: "Before a great war, everyone lies." This is truly the most appropriate explanation of the so-called "peace" in the capitalist world.

Especially at present, the third phase of the capitalist economic panic has broken the balance of power among the powers, making them all feel the terror and sorrow of the imminent end. Therefore, the world is loudly shouting: "War! Only war is the way out of panic!" From such a cause-and-effect relationship, is Japan's act of aggression accidental? Is the world's wait-and-see attitude accidental? Understanding this, do we still have room to appeal to others for peace? Moreover, even if we hope for peace, it should be "upholding justice to achieve peace," and we must never "sacrifice justice for peace." For a year, we have been appealing for peace every day, as if anything can be discussed as long as we can have "peace." Frankly speaking, we do not need such peace. We believe that the establishment of "true peace" must still go through a great battle of total mobilization worldwide.

Winter Sketches

Seasonal Climate and Superstitions

— Yu Dafu

"Tianjia Wuxing" (Farmers' Five Elements) is a precious book for farmers in the countryside of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Some of the rules about the winter climate and superstitions are copied below.

Snow in December indicates a bountiful harvest in the coming year. Rain on the third day indicates prolonged overcast weather, and it will be difficult to get sunny weather in winter and spring. The third "xu" day after the Winter Solstice is the Laba Festival (according to the lunar calendar, this year's Winter Solstice is on November 25, and the third "xu" day is December 26). Three or two snowfalls before and after the Laba Festival are called "three whites before Laba," which is good for vegetables and wheat. It is said that "if you want wheat, see three whites." It is also said that "Laba snow is a bad omen, spring snow is a ghost." And also, "if you see three whites in January, the farmers will laugh heartily." If the snow stops but doesn't melt, it is called "snow waiting for a companion," indicating that there will be more snow. If there is a lot of southeast wind after Laba, it indicates a great flood in the coming year. The same is true for predicting the New Year if the Beginning of Spring (lichun) has not yet occurred.

December 12th is the birthday of silkworms. In Jiaxing and Huzhou, gods are worshipped on this day.

The 24th is called Little New Year. Families in the Wu region must worship the Kitchen God, which is said to be the meaning of bidding farewell to the kitchen. New Year's Eve should be quiet. It is recorded that if dogs do not bark on New Year's Eve, there will be no plague in the coming year. According to folklore, there are plague envoys who descend to the human world to spread plague on that night, so it is advisable to write "The plague has passed, the envoy must know" on yellow paper and post it on the door frame.

December is called the Great Banning Month. If there is a slightly warmer day, it is the omen of Great Cold. There is a saying, "One day with bare arms, three days of shivering."

The folk sayings about the climate of the nine-nine days after the Winter Solstice are: "The first nine and second nine, hands don't leave sleeves. The third nine and twenty-seven, blow the flute on the fence. The fourth nine and thirty-six, the clothes look like dew. The fifth nine and forty-five, the sun opens the door (another saying is, 'a drill or knife cannot enter the soil,' and another saying is, 'the poor man dances in the street'). The sixth nine and fifty-four, the poor boy gets his wish (another saying is, 'tender branches grow on the fence'). The seventh nine and sixty-two, carry cloth sleeves on your shoulder. The eighth nine and seventy-two, a (greasy) dog looks for a shady place. The ninth nine and eighty-one, plows and harrows all come out."

Calculating the seasonal climate from the Winter Solstice seems to be a habit of Eastern astronomers. In China, it is said that a hundred and six days after the Winter Solstice is Qingming (Pure Brightness), while in Japan, it is said that there will be storms on the 210th and 220th days. When the Yuan Dynasty conquered Japan, the entire army was wiped out, probably because they encountered the storm of the 210th and 220th days.

Snow

— Qin

White snow tightly presses down on the earth, and the world trembles in the cold; but, do you believe? Thick spring is already brewing within the snow.

The Monkey and the Whip (Fable)

— Da Ling

After playing in human society for a long time, a monkey returned to his old home, the barren forest of Huaguo Mountain, and brought back many things, one of which was a leather whip that he had stolen.

By the power of this leather whip, he conquered all the other monkeys living in this barren forest. They had to obey his will: to gather fruit for him, to fill his private treasury with gold and silver, to tidy up his bed, to prepare his drinks, to catch fleas on his body, and to fight with neighboring monkeys to protect his territory. And he, then, either sat high on a branch watching for his own amusement, or enjoyed himself hugging a very beautiful female monkey. If he was slightly displeased, he would mercilessly whip them with all his strength. They were slaves to him every day without rest.

Moreover, the monkey holding the whip became more and more ferocious day by day. The other monkeys did not have time to collect food for themselves. When night came, they had no choice but to endure hunger and exhaustion, collapsing randomly on the damp, muddy ground, waiting for the next day's whip and work.

Pain was thus spread throughout this barren forest.

One evening, a monkey who was too tired to die complained to his wife...

"As long as that rascal doesn't have the whip in his hand, he's really not scary. When the whip is still in his hand, although we feel a kind of terror and intense pain, there's no way we can't obey him!"

His smarter female monkey said:

"That rascal must not feel the terror of that ghostly whip!" Her man replied:

"That's what I think too, but I don't understand why."

The female monkey pondered for a moment, then said:

"Could it be because the handle of that ghostly whip is in his hand?"

From that day on, the smart female monkey's powerful words slowly spread among the monkeys in this barren forest. So, one day, they could no longer bear it, so they all moved together and snatched the leather whip from the ferocious monkey's hand, letting the end of the whip dance on his back.

In this way, the monkeys were able to spend time gathering food for themselves and live a peaceful and free life forever. There was no one to oppress them anymore. Moreover, they learned a valuable lesson from this, which is:

"The leather whip must be held for just purposes."

Long Novel

Crossroads of the Times and Love (Manuscript Continued)

— Zhang Ziping

She looked at his sleeping face again, feeling more and more that it was bewitching. Her whole body seemed to be a little hot. She suddenly had an impulse, and brought her smooth lips to his forehead. In just an instant, she moved them to Haiquan's reddish-brown lips. She smelled a kind of odor unique to men.

"If he suddenly sits up, it'll be terrible!"

She was worried about this in her mind, but in reality, she hoped that he would wake up.

But she was still disappointed. He only reached out from the blanket and gently wiped his lips, then turned over to the inside and continued to sleep soundly.

(18)

When Haiquan woke up from his dream, the morning light was already shining in through the window. Because Mrs. Ren had poured him a few glasses of wine last night, he felt a slight pain inside his head when he got up this morning. Seeing that it was getting late, he hurriedly put on his clothes.

"Mr. Lin is awake?"

Just as his left foot was about to go into his slippers, he heard the door of the room creak open, and Mrs. Tsuruko walked in with a smile on her face. As soon as he saw Mrs. Tsuruko, his face darkened.

"Oh dear, Mr. Lin is still angry! I don't know what to do!"

Haiquan wanted to retort to her, why was that Japanese guy still staying in this house? But on second thought, he felt that he really didn't have this right.

"Are you going to school today too?"

She stood to one side, her attitude seeming a little cautious. This made him feel a little bad.

"EH."

He only answered with this sound, and there was still no smile on his face.

"Mr. Lin, if you're not going to school, I'd like to accompany you to have fun outside for a day. There are also many things I want to talk to you about." Mrs. Tsuruko said with a smile.

"Who would accompany you Orientals out?"

Haiquan himself didn't understand why his attitude towards her would be so rude.

"Oh dear! I mean, just me alone will accompany you out!"

Mrs. Tsuruko looked like she was about to cry.

"Don't you have guests at home? You should accompany him."

Haiquan was afraid that she didn't know that he hated that Japanese guy, and he couldn't help but say it out loud in a high-pitched voice.

"Never mind him. They will sit at home, because they have just arrived in Shanghai and don't know the way to Hongkou. I took them around for two or three days, and I was exhausted and annoyed. Who still wants to take care of their affairs! Now he knows the way too. I don't want to accompany them anymore, so that people outside know I'm Japanese!..."

Hearing Mrs. Tsuruko say this, Haiquan couldn't help but be surprised, and at the same time he felt a little pleasure, slightly recovering his cold attitude.
